1 About EQTC Welcome to EQTC! <!--image:traders.jpg-->Welcome!<p>EQTraders Corner (EQTC) was created at the launch of EQ by a stubborn redhead named Niami DenMother (aka 'Mum), in an attempt to make sense of the often-bewildering world of EverQuest tradeskills. </p>
<p>Since it was launched in March 1999, there have been many changes to tradeskills as well as to this website. We've gone from being run on 'Mum's personal AOL webspace to a several million hits per month website and message board setup. We've gone from flat files tracking a few recipes and some vendor and mob drop information to multiple database tables tracking thousands of recipes, mobs, drops and so forth.</p>
<p>One thing hasn't changed, though. We're still privately owned and run by 'Mum (with the technical help of her husband and some phenomenal volunteer staff, led by Aanuvane). Why is this point important? It means that this is basically a labor of love. It's not some huge profit-making site. There is no premium membership. There are no annoying popups. There is no begging in your mailbox asking you to help keep us running. There's just this dedicated staff trying to make sure that tradeskill information is freely available to all and sundry.</p>
<p>We finally broke down and added targeted banner ads to the sites to help pay for them. Just a little extra space taken at the top/bottom of the page. Easy to ignore if you want. {grins}  Running the two sites is a pretty time-consuming, and bandwidth-consuming process these days, and donations alone generally don't do the trick.</p>
<p>We do try, very hard, to ensure that the ads that go through block things like plat sales sites and suchforth, but once in a while one slips through our filters. If you see any ad of questionable legality, please post in our forums so we can get it blocked ASAP.</p>
<p>Please be aware that we do strongly monitor and moderate our message boards, and make sure to read the posts in the Visitor's Corner section of the forums before posting. While the tradeskill information on the site is freely available to all, we DO enforce rules of conduct on those posting to the message boards, and we can/will ban folks from posting if they can't accept our "our house, our rules" decision for the forums. We've seen too many message board forums turn into total chaos, and we're not going to let it happen here - especially now that we have SOE devs regularly stopping in to check on things, based on our reputation for relative sanity. ;)</p>
<p></p>
<p><i>Image above provided/created by <a href="http://www.wtfcomics.com" target="_new">J. Waller of WTF Comics</a></i></p>

<p>Obligatory legalese:  <b>"FTC guidelines require that we disclose to you that Niami DenMother's RL husband is an employee of SOE.  Nonetheless, the opinions and other posts expressed here are those of the EQtraders staff and not of anyone at SOE."</b></p> XXX 2014-10-22 12:10:43 2003-07-16 08:49:50 Niami Denmother 0 0 2014-10-22 12:08:14 Niami Denmother
190 about_pricing Everything You Always Wanted to Know About Merchant Pricing, but were Afraid to Ask <i>by Balidil Anla'shok</i><p>
            <p align="left"><b>Charisma and Faction</b></p>
            <p align="left">As far as vendor prices are concerned, factions can
              be broken up into three categories. Dubious or worse, apprehensive,
              and indifferent or better. If your faction with the merchant is
              dubious or worse, of course, the merchant simply won't sell to you
              (I have something here that %Rs use..let me see...it's the EXIT,
              now get LOST!). If you're
              at apprehensive, the merchant will sell to you, but is going to
              charge you an arm and a leg unless you can get your charisma WAY
              up there. Lastly, any faction indifferent or better will get
              exactly the same prices for the same charisma. It doesn't matter if
              you're ally or sneaking and indifferent. <br>
              There are several crucial charisma numbers to shoot for. Key to
              this is that, whether your faction is apprehensive or indifferent
              or better, there's a stretch from 61 or 62 to 76 or 77 (I haven't
              been able to get a gear combination that gives any of my characters
              either 61 or 76 charisma yet, unfortunately) that gives
              exactly the same prices.  So, if you can get your charisma up to
              62, don't bother getting any more charisma boosters until you can
              get enough to get you to 76. However, when you do get to 76,
              the prices will suddenly drop by about 6%, instead of the 0.5%
              you get for most individual points of charisma. <br>
              Better known is the "magic number" of charisma, 104. This is the
              point at which indifferent or better merchants will give you the
              best price they're ever going to give you. This price seems to be
              based on 1.05 times a "actual value" that you will never see used,
              but is only directly known by the server. For instance, many gem
              and metal prices are clearly based on this. And, if you notice the
              prices at which the vendor will buy such things back from you,
              although it looks like a very irregular number, for instance 95pp
              2gp 3sp 8cp for a bar of platinum or a sapphire, that just happens
              to be 100pp divided by 1.05. <br>
              The last and highest number to shoot for is 132. This is the
              charisma at which you can normally get the cheapest prices even
              with apprehensive faction.</p>

            <p align="left"><b>"Greedy" Merchants</b></p>
            <p align="left"></p>
            <ul>
              <li>Naresa Sparkle?West Commonlands</li>
              <li>Boomba the Big?West Freeport</li>
              <li>Ping Fuzzlecutter?West Freeport</li>
              <li>Tubal Weaver?North Qeynos</li>
              <li>Everyone?The Overthere</li>
            </ul>

            <p align="left"><b>The Pricing Roller Coaster</b></p>
            <p align="left">When many players have been buying from or selling to
              a merchant, he seems to get it into his head that "Hey, I'm so
              popular, I can charge better prices now!". Unfortunately, "better" in
              this context means "better for the vendor". I'm still carrying out
              research on this issue, but merchants that will normally give best
              prices at 104 charisma and indifferent faction can go at least as
              high as needing 134 charisma to get best prices, even with ally
              faction. It seems that, with less charisma than that needed for
              best prices, a set amount is added to the price you would normally
              get, i.e. whether your charisma is 120 or 50, a vendor might add
              3sp to the price you would pay from a vendor who hasn't been getting
              so much action. The actual amount can vary widely. <br>
	      This is particularly noticeable on merchants in very busy areas, for 
	      instance vendors located in or right at the entrance to newbie areas, 
	      or those in banks. In these cases, it's almost impossible to 
	      distinguish a "greedy" merchant from a merely "opportunistic" 
	      merchant. </p>

            <p align="left"><b>Stacking and Prices</b></p>
            <p align="left">When buying or selling items by the stack, the cost can
              be a bit more precise than the single item cost times 20. This can go
              either way, making it more or less efficient to buy or sell by the
              stack. One classic example is water, and other common items that are
              bought for 1sp. Since the real cost is 1sp and 1/2cp, even though the
              per item cost is rounded off to 1sp, when you buy a whole stack at
              once you pay 2gp 1sp, a whole 1sp more than buying them one by one. 
              On the other hand, with my Iksar's rather low charisma, he gets
              shuriken for 1sp 3cp each, but if he buys a stack, he only pays
              2gp 5sp 9cp, and saves a whole copper! <br>
              In general, to the best of my knowledge, this can never make more
              of a difference than 1sp per stack. So I usually don't bother with
              it myself, and just buy my water etc. by the stack. 2005-09-12 11:23:48 2003-06-15 07:27:25 Verdandi Board Goddess 0 0 2005-09-12 11:22:12 Verdandi Board Goddess

11 Alchemy - FAQ Alchemy Frequently Asked Questions <p><i>This FAQ originated on the now-closed Belgar's Alchemy site.  It has been updated and adapted here with permission.</i></p>

<p class="headers">Frequently Asked Questions</p>
<p>
<b>Who can make potions with alchemy?</b>
</p>
<blockquote> <p>Alchemy is a shaman-only skill.</p>
</blockquote>
<p>
<b>When can I start working on alchemy?</b>
</p>
<blockquote> 
<p>
You can start once your shaman is level 25.
</p>
</blockquote>
<p>
<b>Is there a skill cap on alchemy?</b>
</p>
<blockquote> 
<p>
No, but there used to be.  As of the Dragons of Norrath expansion, you can take alchemy all the way to 300 skill at level 25.  Given the cost of ingredients, this would be extremely hard without considerable help; still, it is possible.
</p>
</blockquote>

<p><b>Where can I buy herbs?</b></p>

<blockquote> <p>See our <a href="<!--server:x-->sources/source_trade_page.php?st=Alchemy&menustr=110020000000">Herb Vendors</a> guide for a complete list of known herb vendors throughout Norrath.</p></blockquote>

<p><b>Where do I find the recipes for known alchemy potions?</b></p>

<blockquote> <p>See our <a href="<!--server:x-->recipes/recipe_page.php?article=29&rsa=Alchemy&sb=item&sub=&menustr=080010000000">Alchemy Recipes</a> pages for detailed recipes and effects.</p> </blockquote>

<p><b>What are the best potions to make in order to increase my alchemy skill?</b></p>

<blockquote><p>We're working on revising this answer, as it's changed considerably since the last edit.</p></blockquote>

<p><b>What attribute has the greatest effect on alchemy success rates and skill increases?</b></p>

<blockquote> <p>Wisdom. </p>
<p>See our guide on <a href="<!--server:x-->articles/article_page.php?article=g8&menustr=040010000000">Beginning Alchemy</a> for more information.</p> </blockquote>

<p><b>Where do I find the various dropped ingredients used for certain alchemy potions?</b></p>
<blockquote> <p>Search for the item or click on it in a recipe.  Part of the item detail is the known sources, including what can drop it and where it is foraged.  If you cannot yet kill the kind of creature that drops an ingredient, or cannot easily get to them, try checking vendors near those creatures to see if players have sold some off. </p> </blockquote>

<p><b>What is the air-speed velocity of an unladen swallow?</b></p>

<blockquote><p>An intriguing and age-old question that is highly dependent upon whether one is speaking of the African swallow, or the European swallow. See Monty Python's "The Search for the Holy Grail" for further details.</p></blockquote> 2006-09-18 10:48:26 2003-05-14 01:20:02 Verdandi Board Goddess 0 1 2010-12-06 08:27:14 EQTC Editor Aanuvane
8 Alchemy - Getting Started Alchemy: Getting Started <p><i>This guide originated on the now-closed Belgar's Alchemy site. It has been adapted and updated here with permission.</i></p>

<p>So you wanna make potions for fun and profit? Well, maybe just for fun anyway. Here's a suggested step by step way to get your new skill started.</p>

<p class="headers">The Skill Cap:</p>

<p>The only restrictions on alchemy are that only shamans can do it, and they must be level 25 to start.  Alchemy <i>used to</i> also be capped at five points of skill per level.  That has changed, so that a shaman at level 25 can go all the way to 300 skill.</p>

<p>The trainer at any shaman guild will allow you to put 21 initial practice points into alchemy skill, but no more. This is true whether or not you actually put any training points in before 21.  Skill above that level must be obtained "in the field", which means to get further skill increases above 21 you will need to attempt to make potions. So unless you'd prefer to spend considerable time and/or plat getting there the hard way, I recommend saving 21 guild practice points to start your alchemy off. </p>

<p class="headers"> The Influence of Stats:</p> 

<p>Originally the popular theory was that intelligence helped you gain skill faster, while wisdom helped you successfully create items more often. <b>This is incorrect.</b>  For alchemy, it is either the highest of your intelligence or your wisdom that determines how quickly your skill improves.  Given that shamans need wisdom for our spell casting, and have no use for intelligence whatsoever, you can ignore intelligence and focus on wisdom.</p>

<p>Only your skill (and certain AA abilities), and not any stat, determines how often you succeed at making something.   For more on this, see the <a href="http://mboards.eqtraders.com/eq/showthread.php?t=19">Stats and Tradeskills FAQ</a>. </p>

<p class="headers">New to Tradeskills?</p> 

<p>The basic system of tradeskills is that you have certain ingredients which are combined in a certain tradeskill container.  For example, to make a Distillate of Alacrity I, get one Arnworth, five small vials and a medicine bag.  When you first open the medicine bag, it may open to a window that looks just like any other container, except with a Combine button in addition to the Done button.  Or, it may be more complex, with a search interface and buttons for "favorite recipes" and an Experiment button.  That is the recipe book, which lets you create things more quickly, by automatically combining the right ingredients when you select that recipe in the "book".  The catch is that not all recipes are available in your recipe book to start.  Some of them you will have to make once to learn them, after which they will be in your recipe book.</p>

<p>So if you want to use the recipe book to make a Distillate of Alacrity I, search for Distillate of Alacrity.  Then select it in the result list box and hit Combine.  It will automatically find the right six ingredients in your inventory and attempt the combine for you.</p>

<p>If you would rather use the experiment mode, or are attempting a recipe that you need to learn first, open the container in experiment mode and put the five ingredients in.  Remember that multiple quanties of the same item must be placed into each slot unstacked in order to perform the combine.  Click combine to attempt the combine.</p>

<p>Whichever way you choose to attempt your combine, you will receive one of five possible messages and success/failure outcome combinations</p>

<blockquote> 
<p>a) You fail and receive a message indicating <u>you do not have the skill</u> to make that potion. (This message is the same when you fail, regardless of your actual skill relative to the recipe difficulty.)</p>
<p>b) You will fail but receive a message indicating <u>your skill in alchemy has increased</u>. (One of the best messages!)</p>
<p>c) You will succeed> in making the potion and receive a message indicating <u>you have created something new</u>, but receive no indication of whether the potion is trivial.  (That means it is not trivial yet.)</p>
<p>d) You will succeed> in making the potion and receive a message indicating <u>your skill in alchemy has increased</u>. (Twice as good!)</p>
<p>e) You will succeed in making the potion and receive a message indicating that <u>you can no longer advance in skill from making this item</u>.  (That means that recipe is trivial to you, so that you can no longer improve your skill by making it.)</p>
</blockquote> XXX 2010-11-27 12:00:14 2003-05-14 01:13:13 EQTC Editor Aanuvane 0 1 2015-01-02 01:23:27 EQTC Editor Aanuvane
9 Alchemy - History Alchemy: A Not-so-Brief History <p class="headers">by Verdandi Snowblood</p>
            
<p>In the beginning, there were two kinds of herb vendors. One was found in some shaman cities and had a set of herbs that each could be combined with a different dropped item, like a cyclops eye or undead froglok tongue. The other type of vendor was the gypsies, found in gypsy camps across Antonica. They had a different, smaller set of herbs that each also could be combined with a different kind of dropped giant toe to make other potions.</p>

<p>However, shaman guild trainers across Norrath refused to train their pupils in the fine art of alchemy. It was well nigh a year before they received their instructions from The Powers That Be and began to teach us the fundamentals of alchemy.  The herbs and potions at the time were extremely expensive and of very limited usefulness. (One of them with an herb cost of more than 30pp and requiring a drop from the Plane of Hate had the tremendous effect of Endure Magic.) Therefore, when our guildmasters were fixed so that we could train, our line of potions available was completely replaced with new ones. This change is commonly called the Revamp.</p>

<p>All of the old shaman city vendor herbs were removed entirely, effectively removing access to those potions. Only the gypsy vendors remained and their potions continued to work. In the cities, the old herb vendors were replaced by a whole new set of herbs that took up two vendors because there were so many. These are the herbs that are most familiar to folks nowadays, the ones that can make sow potions and invis to undead potions. For these potions, no dropped component is required, they are made entirely via herbs bought from the vendors.</p>

<p>Thus the world remained, with Revamp Alchemy and Gypsy Alchemy composing almost the entire line of alchemy available. During the Revamp era we were granted the ability to create dyes for use in tinting fine plate armor. However, as these can only be applied to that single type of armor, they are not widely used.</p>

<p>With the advent of Luclin two additional sets of potions were added to a shaman's menu. First was a whole new set of potions with brand new effects. These include the mana potions and grow potion. These herbs are available in a few different places, all in Luclin. The other set of potions...well, shamans exploring Shar Vahl came across these strange herbs with naggingly familiar names...until it hit them. Old Alchemy. Once again available, this time in Shar Vahl, are the herbs used to make potions from the old, original, pre-revamp alchemy. These are the ones that required the drops like cyclops eyes and undead froglok tongues. </p>

<p>The discovery of the Plane of Knowledge brought only a single additional recipe for shamans, Quintessence of Knowledge, used as a reagent for a couple new items available in the new Planes. Some time after we ventured into the new Planes, we also learned to create the Grandmaster's Medicine Bag as a trophy of our accomplishments and useful reward for our hard work.</p>

<p>Most recently, the Ykesha brought us a diverse wealth of additional potions. Some of these grant the illusion of a different race, some grant new focus effects, some allow the creation of dyes effective on any armor, and some bring new effects similar to those we had in previous lines of alchemy, including gating to one's bind spot or group shrink. Some of these use vendor ingredients found only in the Ykesha zones, some require dropped ingredients, some require herbs from Revamp alchemy, and some require a combination of all these sources. Truly a mixed bag.</p>

<p>The Lost Dungeons of Norrath, or LDoN, introduced five new alchemy potions.  Three of them are the first group effect potions.  Another is the first shaman-made invisibility potion, allowing us to compete with the invisibility potion sold by vendors since the beginning.  The fifth is the guktan illusion potion, complementing the introduction of the playable guktan race.</p> 

<p>When Gates of Discord came, we received two new lines of potions: awareness potions and concoctions.  Awareness potions offer focus effects for different types of spells.  Concoctions can be equipped and thrown as missiles, with varying effects like snare or damage.  We also received the quests to learn to process taelosian sludge and highland fudge, part of the larger set of processing quests available in all tradeskills.  Neither of the sludges have any known use at this time.</p>

<p>One of the latest and greatest items made with alchemy are the Omens of War augments.  These beauties require some rare and difficult drops, but create some fantastic items.  The complete process of creation also requires jewelcraft, and can be done by rogues with poisonmaking rather than shamans with alchemy.  Still, a fantastic option.</p>

<p>Most recently, Dragons of Norrath brought a hodgepodge of potions. Some are additions to the awareness lines of potions, including some with effects like regeneration, rather than focus effects.  There are also additions to the concoctions lines, and a way of bottling both DoN and previous concoctions to enhance their effects further.</p>

<p>Thus, the major lines of alchemy are:</p>
<ol>
<li>Old Alchemy (requires dropped ingredients, herbs only found in Shar Vahl)</li>
<li>Gypsy Alchemy (requires dropped ingredients, herbs only found on gypsies)</li>
<li>Revamp Alchemy (no dropped ingredients, herbs found in many places)</li>
<li>Luclin Alchemy (no dropped ingredients, herbs found only on Luclin)</li>
<li>Quintessence of Knowledge & Grandmaster's Medicine Bag</li>
<li>Ykesha Alchemy (some require drops and some don't, herb vendors vary by type of potion)</li>
<li>LDoN Alchemy (some revamp alchemy ingredients, some foraged ingredients)</li>
<li>GoD Alchemy (no dropped ingredients for concotions, only to process sludge, which has no known use)</li>
<li>Omens Augments (requires dropped ingredients, no herbs but other ingredients off varying vendors)</li>
<li>Dragons Alchemy (requires dropped ingredients, herbs found in various places)</li>
</ol> 2010-11-27 12:01:38 2003-05-14 01:30:30 EQTC Editor Aanuvane 0 1 2010-11-27 12:14:14 EQTC Editor Aanuvane
10 Alchemy - Tools Alchemy: Tools & Accessories <p><b><i>Bags:</i></b> Click the name of the vendor or crafted items to be taken to the purchasing information or recipe.</p>

<ul>
<li><b><!--item_ulinkedname:1141--></b> - <i>Vendor bought</i>, this fundamental alchemy tool is the container in which you combine your ingredients.  Every single alchemy recipe uses a medicine bag. They are available from most alchemy vendors, especially those carrying a large selection of herbs.</li>

<li><b><!--item_ulinkedname:8268--></b> - This is a <i>tailored</i> alternative to the Medicine Bag.  They are more expensive and more difficult to acquire but much easier to store between uses.  The item itself is not a container and can therefore be stored in any bags that can hold small items.  In order to get the usable container, you put the Folded Medicine Bag in one of your general inventory slots and right click it.  This will summon a Folding Medicine Bag, a No Drop container that is functionally identical to the vendor-sold Medicine Bag.  It is not No Rent.  Your Folded Medicine Bag remains in your possession after you have summoned the Folding Medicine Bag.  Therefore, when you are done with the summoned Folding Medicine Bag, you can delete it.  Just be careful to delete the summoned Folding bag rather than the Folded bag.</li>

<li><b><!--item_ulinkedname:1824--></b> - This <i>tailored</i> bag is the basic tool for creating potions that have 5 or 10 charges.  To use, combine either 5 or 10 single charges of the same potion into the bag.  This process will never fail but will never give you any further skill.  Because it never fails, anyone can use this bag, even those who are not practicing alchemists or even shamans.  The Bearskin Potion Bag is a container capable of holding tiny or small items.</li>

<li><b><!--item_ulinkedname:8270--></b> - A <i>tailored</i> alternative to the Bearskin Potion bag, this item works much like the Folded Medicine Bag.  They are a little more expensive and harder to make but much easier to store between uses.  The item itself is not a container and can therefore be stored in any bags that can hold small items.  In order to get the usable container, you put the Folded Bearskin Potion Bag in one of your general inventory slots and right click it.  This will summon a Folding Bearskin Potion Bag, a No Drop container that is functionally identical to the regular Bearskin Potion Bag.  It is not No Rent.  Your Folded Bearskin Potion Bag remains in your possession after you have summoned the Folding Bearskin Potion Bag.  Therefore, when you are done with the summoned Folding Bearskin Potion Bag, you can delete it.  Just be careful to delete the summoned Folding bag rather than the Folded bag.</li>
</ul>

<br>
<p><b><i>Skill Modifiers:</i></b>  Click the name of the crafted items to be taken to the recipe.  Note that these items do NOT stack with one another.  When you equip more than one alchemy modifying item at a time, only the highest percentage item will affect your alchemy skill.  Also note that equipping any one of these items only affects your changes of success.  For the purposes of trivials, your actual skill is still what determines whether or not you can skill up off of that item and whether or not you receive a trivial message upon success.  For example, if your alchemy skill is 100 and you have this item equipped, you will have the same chance of success as someone with a skill of 105.  However, you will still be able to improve your skill by practicing with recipes that trivial from 101-105.  Whether or not you receive a trivial message will also be determined by the trivial of the potion compared to your actual skill, and ignores the effect of the skill modifying item.</p>

<ul>
<li><b><!--item_ulinkedname:8272--></b>:  This item is created by gnomes via <i>tinkering</i>. When equipped it grants a 5% bonus to your alchemy skill. </li>

<li><b>Alchemist Trophies:</b>  With the Prophecy of Ro expansion, the tradeskill trophies were revamped.  Now, aspiring trade skill masters can obtain quests from Baublie Diggs in the West Freeport newbie area to obtain an initial trophy that is commensurate with their current skill.  As combines to increase skill are continue, the trophy will evolve providing increasing bonuses to the tradeskiller's skill.  Additionally, these trophies will also summon no rent bags.

<ul><li><b><!--item_ulinkedname:23002--></b>:  Provides a 1% bonus to your alchemy skill and will summon a Beginner Artisan Satchel.</li>

<li><b><!--item_ulinkedname:23003--></b>:  Provides a 2% bonus to your alchemy skill and will summon an Apprentice Artisan Satchel.</li>

<li><b><!--item_ulinkedname:23004--></b>:  Provides a 4% bonus to your alchemy skill and will summon a Freshman Artisan Satchel. </li>

<li><b><!--item_ulinkedname:23005--></b>:  Provides a 5% bonus to your alchemy skill and will summon a Journeyman Artisan Satchel. </li>

<li><b><!--item_ulinkedname:23006--></b>: Provides an 8% bonus to your alchemy skill and will summon an Expert Artisan Satchel. </li>

<li><b><!--item_ulinkedname:23007--></b>: Provides a 12% bonus to your alchemy skill and will summon a Master Artisan Satchel. </li>

<li><b><!--item_ulinkedname:23008--></b>: Provides a 15% bonus to your alchemy skill and will summon an Artisan Satchel. </li></ul>

<li><b>Philosopher's Stone</b>:  <b>This item can no longer be obtained, except from other players.</b>  It adds 10% to your alchemy skill.  It used to come from the Alchemist Varona in Grieg's End, but she no longer spawns.</li>

<li><b>Umbracite Swarm Orb</b>:  This <i>dropped</i> item is from Vex Thal and adds a whopping 15% to your alchemy skill, as well as <a href="http://everquest.allakhazam.com/db/item.html?item=12413">a whole slew of other stats</a>. It is No Trade.</li>
</ul> 2010-11-27 10:40:23 2003-05-03 07:58:02 EQTC Editor Aanuvane 0 1 2016-05-01 07:24:25 EQTC Editor Aanuvane

558 EQTC:Learn:TailoringNEW NEW! Tailoring Skill Up Guide <p>Ok so the stuff I'm about to post below isn't technically *new*.  It's been around for a long time in one fashion or another over in the EQ Traders Forums.  I'm just transcribing it here so it might be easier for newer folks to find.</P>

<p>If you have zero skill in Tailoring, the first thing you should do is go to Crescent Reach and see Tailor Nabirye.  She's on the second floor of Crescent Reach with the other Tailoring Vendor and Quest NPCs.  From her, you can obtain a set of "freebie" Tailoring tasks that will raise your tailoring skill to 54.  Hint:  You don't get noticable experience or faction gain from doing these tasks, so just keep asking for supplies and make more items until you hit the trivial for the item she has asked you to make.  Then you can either turn 20 of the item in or delete the quest and get the next one.  There is also a "freebie" type quest offered in Abysmal Sea.  It's a little different and not quite as refined as the CR freebies are.</p>

<p>After you've gotten your skill to 54, immediately head over to West Freeport and see Baublie Diggs for the Beginner Tailor Test (<a href="<!--server:x-->articles/article_page.php?article=q233&menustr=040110000000">Trophy Quests</a> for more info).  Gather the ingredients up, make the items, turn them in and get your trophy.  Though this won't modify your tailoring skill much at this point, always keep it equipped when you're doing combines so it evolves with your skill level.  Eventually it will give you a nice skill mod.  You can wait and get one of the other trophy tasks, but be warned:  The higher the "test" the more difficult it becomes to obtain the ingredients to make the items in the test.<p>

<p>From this point you have lots of different paths you can choose.  Personally, if your only goal is to skill up as quickly as possible, I recommend sticking with Silk and Leather glove templates.  The silks and pelts aren't super hard to come by either by farming, barter or vendor diving depending on your available platinum reserves.  There's an alternative route of Hilt Wraps, but those will only get you to 268 (technically you can go to 282, but the higher pelts have better uses) and can only be done with pelts.<p>

<p>Glove Template Patterns:</p>

204 EQTC:Learn:Xref:loy_research Cross-Reference: LoY Spell Research Drops <p>This is a list of the pages, runes, words, and other components needed for researching 50+ spells, designed to help figure out what drops are worth keeping and roughly what they're worth.  In the parenthesis after each spell name is the first letter of the class, and the level at which that class can use it.  Thus, (M55) denotes a level 55 mage spell, while (S59) is a level 59 shaman spell.  Components that can be used to <a href="<!--server:x-->recipes/recipe_page.php?article=125&rsa=Spell%20Research&sub=other&sb=item&menustr=080105120000">tailor robes</a> have the name of the swatch they produce noted after the spells.</p>
<p>Where drops have a ? before and after the name, they were only listed in the recipes for priest class spells and not for the int caster spells.  I'm not sure yet if they are mistakes in game or if something got goofed when they were translated on the boards for us, so take those with a grain of salt.  Also, the 60 cleric spell Blessing of Aegolism was listed with the same component twice in the recipe, so in practice it probably requires at least one more thing that's not noted for it here. Lastly, quite frankly my eyes started to glaze over as I plowed through the sea of yaeths and words and runes and toharons and zeannors, so there are probably mistakes of my own doing.  If you find any, please just point em out on the <a href="http://mboards.eqtraders.com/phpBB2/viewforum.php?f=79">message boards</a> and I'll get em fixed.</p>

            <table cellpadding="2" hspace="10" bordercolor="#400000"
vspace="1" border="2" cellspacing="0">
              <tr bgcolor="#E3E4D3"> 
                <td> <p align=center class="headers">Drop</td>
                <td> <p align=center class="headers">Spells It Makes (class, level 
                    of use)</td>
              </tr>
              <tr bgcolor="#E3E4D3"> 
                <td class="intable" colspan="2"> <p align=center> <b><i>Pages</i></b></td>
              </tr>
              <tr> 
                <td class="intable">finnok's 2 left</td>
                <td class="intable">spirit of the howler (S55), zumaik's animation 
                  (E55), hammer of judgement (C56), hammer of divinity (C58), 
                  hammer of souls (C60)</td>
              </tr>

                <td class="intable">finnok's 2 right</td>
                <td class="intable">zumaik's animation (E55)</td>
              </tr>

                <td class="intable">keris's 5 left</td>
                <td class="intable">color slant (E52)</td>

205 EQTC:Learn:Xref:old_research Cross-Reference: Old Spell Research Drops <p>These are the pages, runes, words, and other components needed for researching level 1-49 spells, with a list of what can be made from each.  It is intended to as a guide for researchers who want a quick reference for what items they should save, and for both researchers and non-researchers who want to know the value of the research items they find.  This list includes some ingredients that are also available from vendors as well as items that are drops only.  See the <a href="<!--server:x-->sources/source_trade_page.php?st=Spell%20Research&menustr=110120000000">Spell Research Trade Supplies</a> list for information on what is available on vendors and where. </p>

<p>Pages can only be used by enchanters while runes can only be used by wizards.  Words, on the other hand, are used by both necromancers and magicians.  None of the same words are used by both classes, so they have been listed with their respective classes so that necros and mages have more tailored lists for their own uses.  The level at which a spell can be used by that class is noted in parenthesis after the spell name.  Components that can be used to <a href="<!--server:x-->recipes/recipe_page.php?article=125&rsa=Spell%20Research&sub=other&sb=item&menustr=080105120000">tailor robes</a> have the name of the swatch they produce noted after the spells.</p>

<p>If you find any mistakes, please point them out on the <a href="http://mboards.eqtraders.com/phpBB2/viewforum.php?f=79">message boards</a> and we'll get em fixed.</p>
            <p align="center"><a href="#enchanter">enchanters</a> -- <a href="#mage">mages</a> 
              -- <a href="#necro">necros</a> -- <a href="#wizzie">wizards</a> 
            </p>
            <table cellpadding="2" hspace="10" bordercolor="#400000"
vspace="1" border="2" cellspacing="0">

              </tr>

Recovering faded pages can fail.</i></td>

<p> 2004-07-09 12:28:31 2003-06-12 08:30:45 Krazick DB Master 0 1 2005-02-11 02:06:34 Niami Denmother
93 EQTC:Links EQTC Links <h3>
  <p align=Left>General EQ links: </p>
</h3>

<p><b>PLEASE NOTE:</b>  Many pages are not being actively maintained at this time and many of these links may be out of date.  Please feel free to report any stale links in the database update forum and we'll make the updates as we have time.</p>

<ul>
  <li><a href="http://www.everquest.com" target="_new">www.everquest.com</a> - Sony's main EQ website contains news of interest to EQ players (scheduled downtime, policy changes, etc.) Also vist their <a href="http://eqlive.station.sony.com/" target="_new">EQ Live site</a> for up-to-the-minute news and announcements.</li>
  <li><a href="http://everquest.allakhazam.com" target="_new">AllaKhazam's Magical Realm</a> is my favorite place to find information on quests and items not covered by our site.They also host Illia's Bestiary and the <a href="http://lucy.allakhazam.com/index.html" target="_new">Lucy item/spell database</a>. </li>
  <li><a href="http://lomonmanor.home.comcast.net/" target="_new">Lomon Manor: Library of Arcane Knowledge</a> - an impressively collection of text from books within Everquest, including all or almost all of the tradeskill texts</li>
  <li> <a href="http://www.eqvault.com/" target="_new">www.eqvault.com </a>- This site contains recent news about the game, player guides, maps and more.</li>
  <li> <a href="http://eq.ogaming.com" target="_new">EQ Ogaming</a> - carries information on quests, abilities and much more.</li>
  <li>Having a hard time tracking your gear? Want to make up a list of your perfect gear? The <a href="http://www.magelo.com" target="_new">Magelo database</a> can help!</li>
  <li>Mum is VERY prone to getting lost in-game. If you're the same way, fear not! EQ-Toolbox has <a href="http://www.mapfiend.net/" target="_new">Map Fiend</a>, which has lots of maps to download for use in-game. Finally, I can find my way out of a paper bag ... and whichever LDoN zone I've roamed into this time!</li>
  <li> At a total loss as to how to set up a custom UI? Looking for pre-made UI mods? <a href="http://eqinterface.com" target="_new">EQ Interface</a> may have what you need.</li>
  <li> Confused over which LDoNs you need to do in order to get what item? Check out this lovely <a href="http://www.cardplace.com/eq/ldon/list.cgi" target="_new">LDoN merchant sorting script</a>.</li>
  <li><a href="http://mywebpages.comcast.net/aoenla/fletchguide/" target="_new">Aoenla's Fletching Guide</a> is no longer updated, but it's still a valuable resource to the fletchers of Norrath </li>
  <li><a href="http://www.everquest-online.com" target="_new">Everquest Online</a> has a search engine for searching for just the right gear, etc.</li>
  <li><a href="http://eq.rpgfashion.com/Everquest/" target="_new">RPG Fashion</a> - mixed in with looted armor fashions are screen shots of player-made gear. (This site is a revamp/relaunch of the EQ Fashion site). </li>
  <li><a href="http://www.eqecon.com/" target="_new">EQ Econ</a> tracks item prices in the bazaar on a per-server basis.</li>
<li><a href="http://www.eqpeople.com/forums/" target="_new">EQ People</a> has message boards for general Everquest and other gaming chat.
<li><a href="http://www.eqprofits.com" target="_new">EQ Profits</a> - Bazaar prices and recommended items and techniques (including tradeskills) to make a profit! Plus personalised trading analysis from your own log fil.</li>
</ul>
<h3>The Lighter Side of Gaming</h3>
<ul>  <li><a href="http://www.gucomics.com" target="_new">GU Comics</a> - everyone needs a dose of humor now and then, and Woody gives us his humorous views of life in (and out) of EQ and other games. (Several images of his are scattered around the site, with his permission.) </li>
  <li><a href="http://www.wtfcomics.com/index.html" target="_new">WTF Comics</a> is an ongoing series of EQ-related comic strips with a large following. Also, <a href="<!--server:x-->articles/article_page.php?article=g375">click here for info on the cameo appearance of Niami and Ngreth on WTF Comics, as well as some custom art that Jeremy created for us.</a></li>
<li><a href="http://www.ctrlaltdel-online.com/index.php" target="_new">CTRL+ALT+DEL</a> is another online comic that we enjoy. Mum's favorite so far, of course, is the one on skilling up baking, IRL!</a>
</ul>
<h3><p align=Left>Class Sites:</h3>
<ul>
  <li><a href="http://therunes.net" target="_new">The Runes</a> is a site for enchanters. </li>
  <li><a href="http://www.eqclerics.org/" target="_new">EQ Cleric</a> for all your clerical questions. </li>
  <li><a href="http://forums.interealms.com/ranger/" target="_new">Rangers Glade</a> forums for the rangers amongst us. </li>
   <li><a href="http://www.thesafehouse.org" target="_new">The Safehouse</a> is a very important and active resource for all the rogues ... erm ... scouts ... out there (as well as being an important haven for several other fan sites). 
  </li>
  <li>For the druids amongst us, try the <a href="http://www.thedruidsgrove.org/" target="_new">Druids Grove.</li>
  <li><a href="http://crucible.samanna.net" target="_new">The Crucible</a> has forums for the shaman and paladin classes</li>
  <li><a href="http://kikyara.tripod.com/" target="_new">Kiky's Poisonous Pages</a> - Kiky has left the lands, and her site is no longer updated, but there's some good information here.<i> (Warning, this is a popup-heavy site)</i></li>
  <li><a href="http://www.conan.ch/eqwar/" target="_new">EverQuest Warrior</a> has several links of interest to EQ warriors</li>
<li><a href="http://www.thesteelwarrior.org/forum/" target="_new">The Steel 
Warrior</a> message boards are a good forum for the tanks among us.</li>
<li><a href="http://eq1.eqsummoners.com" target="_new">The Magician's Tower forums</a> are still going strong.</li>
</ul>
<h3><p align=Left>EQ/gaming in the real world</h3>
<ul>
  <li>Fricka of <a href="http://www.OffLineTshirts.com" target="_new">Off-Line</a> has some lovely RP t-shirts, including some EQ-specific ones ("Got Clarity?")</li>
<li><font color="blue"><b>NEW!</b></font> <a href="http://www.gwydhar.com/statement.shtml">Gwydhar</a> does some fabulous character portraits (amidst all of her other lovely art) if you wish to have one of your favorite characters immortalized. We got to see her in action at the 2008 Fan Faire.</li>
  <li><a href="http://www.nickyee.com/daedalus/" target="_new">The Daedalus Project</a> researches the impact of MMORPGs on our lives.</li>
</ul>
<h3><p align=Left>Other worlds:</h3>
<ul>
  <li><a href="http://everquest2.station.sony.com/" target="_new">EverQuest II</a>, of course, is alive and kicking. </li>
<li><a href="https://www.dcuniverseonline.com/home">DC Universe Online</a> allows you to run amok as a hero or villain in a DC Univese setting</li>
  <li><a href="http://www.darkageofcamelot.com" target="_new">Dark Ages of Camelot</a> is yet another MMORPG that DenMom helped beta test. If you're already playing DAoC, check out: <a href="http://www.camelotherald.com/index.php" target="_new">The Camelot Herald</a>.</li>
<li>If you're into building your community, and your tradeskills from the ground up (or should I say from the flax seed up), see if you can help make the perfect Egyptian community in <a href="http://www.atitd.com/" target="_new">A Tale in the Desert</a>. There isn't any combat, but there's a pretty strong community on <a href="http://wiki.atitd.net/tale3" target="_new">their player-run wiki</a> and their <a href="http://www.atitd.net/forum/" target="_new">player-run forums.</a></li>
</ul>
<h3><p align=Left>Non-gaming Links - the EQTC Community helping 
  the RL world at large</h3>
<ul>
  <li>While grid.org has closed their doors, and Team EQTC is no longer turning CPU time into valuable medical research processing time, the battle is far from over. Check out <b><i><a href=http://www.eqtraders.com/articles/article_page.php?article=g411">the bottom of this article</a></i></b> for details on other grid projects that can help turn previously idle CPU time into valuable research time!</li>
<li><a href="http://www.thehungersite.com">The Hunger Site and Affiliates</a> - just a click a day on these 6 sites helps donate resources to six good causes. Won't you lend a hand?</li>
</ul> XXX 2016-06-27 12:01:26 2003-07-03 11:29:38 Niami Denmother 0 1 2017-12-17 07:16:49 EQTC Editor Aanuvane
206 EQTC:PayPal Help EQ Traders Corner Stay Running and Ad-free!! <table width=\"90%\" border=\"0\">
<tr>
<td>
<!--image_op:gu_20010211.jpg..200..300..0..left-->
</td>
<td> 
<p>
There are many expenses that come with running this site, and as the popularity of EQTC grows, so do the costs. It is no longer feasible for us to pay for the costs by ourselves, so we\'re asking for the help of those in the community who are able to contribute. <i>(FYI: All of the first two years, including domain name registrations, EZBoard fees, software and hardware costs were covered by the DenMother and House Ogre. Since December 2001, we\'ve accepted donations, but they do not cover the growing costs of running this site.)</i> While we\'re thrilled that the site has become so popular, the surge in traffic is really starting to cost money, especially now that it\'s become so costly to keep the message boards free of ads. (Not to mention a solid 60-80 hours a week of combined time from the DenMother and the House Ogre while the database is being built/developed.)
</p> 
<p>
We really <i><b>DO</b></i> want to keep the boards ad-free, and continue to develop the tradeskill database that will make recipe and supply hunting much easier, but we cannot do it without the support of the community.
</p> 
<p>
Currently, we have only the one method for donating to the site, though we may work out a second alternative for those of you who have problems with Paypal accounts for any reason:
</p> 
<p>
<b>Paypal</b> - donations go directly to the DemMother to help cover the new hosting costs, message board costs, software/hardware expenses, etc. If there\'s any left over (there usually isn\'t), it will go to cover things for Niami like asprin, chocolate, massage therapy, ... and hair color to hide the grey hairs that the site has caused ... consider it her \"pay\" for the amount of work put into this site. ;)
</p>
</td>
</tr>
</table> 
<p>
 
</p>

</p>

5 EQTC Editor Krazick The Patch Message I won't repeat the entire patch message, but here are the parts that are relevant to tradeskills, along with some commentary:

<ul><li><b>Added over 1,000 new tradeskill recipes for all levels of skill,</b> along with many recipe books. A few of the vendors of Norrath might be able to get you started on your way <i>(of course, we'll be scrambling here to get the information online for all of you, but expect things to be a tad ... hectic ... for a while) </i></li>
<li>Added Mortar and Pestle to a Thurgadin merchant <i>(this should make poisonmaking, dyemaking, pottery idols, and a few other things a bit easier for those who have chosen to live mostly in Velious)</i></li>
<li>Rubbing Alcohol is now available from a vendor in Thurgadin <i>(happy shawl questing! No more running to Cabilis!)</i></li>
<li>Hit point bonuses on food items should be working <i>(centi steaks and centi toe stew, anyone?) </i></li>
<li>Characters can no longer scribe a scroll that they can't cast due to deity restrictions <i>(imbue gem spells were bugged for a while so anyone of the proper level/class could scribe them, now you should be able to only scribe the spell for your deity)</i></li></ul>
<p>Your best bet for the first 24 hours is to keep an eye on the message boards for the new recipes. It's going to take some time to get these things webbed, especially with the server lag I'm already seeing this morning from eager folks at w*rk hitting the site, trying to see if anything's been found yet. 
<p><b><i>Addendum - </i></b>
<p>Erm, um ... if you tried to access the message boards earlier, and were timing out all over the place, you weren't alone. I feel sort of bad for the folks at EZBoard when they saw the load hit today. We've now been moved to a server of our very own (I'll be sending them a very heartfelt thank you to them for their fast work). The reroute to the new message board server is automagic, but please DO change your bookmarks when you have a chance, to cut down on their load.. It will take me days before I can change all the links on all the pages other than the front page, as the recipes that everyone's trying to get information on are the priority right now. <a href="http://mboards.eqtraders.com/phpBB2/index.php">New message board link</a>
<p>It's going to take a while to get recipes into their proper places, and stuff tested out. There's a temporary recipe page found here, and as things there get verified, tested, etc., I'll get them onto the normal recipe pages as well. 
<p align="right">~DenMom</p> 2002-05-08 06:25:38 2018-12-27 06:24:13 2018-12-27 06:24:05 0 Ngreth Thergn
6 EQTC Editor Krazick Happy Mother's Day! In a very hobbit sort of way (giving gifts on a special day instead of receiving them) this tired mother (of this community, plus 3 cats ;D) has a plethora of gifts for you all. Recipes, recipes everywhere! Yes, it's chaos everywhere, with tradesfolk running around, comparing notes, wanting to exchange their gifts for other gifts, and so on. It's going to take quite a while for things to settle down around here and for "DenMom" to clean up everything. In the meantime, you'll want to watch the message boards (as always), as well as bookmark the following: Main collection of May 8, 2002 recipes, <a href="<!--server:x-->articles/article_page.php?article=g79&menustr=080040120000">wood elven cultural</a>, <a href="<!--server:x-->articles/article_page.php?article=g67&menustr=080040000000">other cultural</a>. Yes, I really do mean to move each of the cultures to their own page for easier sorting out, and then later merge them with their other cultural recipes, but I keep getting sidetracked by new recipe updates. It'll get there.
<p>I've been agonizing for over a day now what to mention in a front page update, as so much of it is newsworthy to varying parts of the tradeskill community, and I know, no matter what I highlight, someone will feel left out. Some posts late last night/early this morning decided me on what would be highlighted ...
<p>Druids and tradeskillers from all across Norrath have been hard at work, deciphering the Liber Brassica Felix books, in search of the Protection of the Cabbage spell (a single-target PoTG). It's been a monumental undertaking, and I'd like to thank the EQTC community and the folks over at the Druid Grove for sharing information and ideas enough to get this sorted out quickly. The quest has been gargantuan, to say the least. And it's now over. The lovely Lady Xanthe Ravenwolf of Bertoxx exhaustedly reported in last night that she had completed the quest, and was kind enough to provide us with information on the reward (the spell and a nice earring), and a run-down of the quest. (I'll be working on webbing it after the caffeine kicks in.) We then received a visit from Rich Waters, one of the Lead Designers from EQ (I swear, he's got to be getting as little sleep as I am right now, from the looks of his posts on the boards!)
<p>Rich said
<p><blockquote>
Congratulations, Xanthe!
<p>With the first completion of this quest, a new spell was brought into the world, and I'd like to thank the many druids and tradesfolk who participated in this event. 
<p>This quest is unusual in EverQuest, as it was intended to be done once and then change after it was solved. In the next patch, Xanthe will reap the rewards of finishing the quest first, and all druids will find the scroll much easier to attain now that the quest has been completed.
<p>The quest will stay in game, for people who enjoy tradeskills and anyone who completes the full quest will find the final reward is quite suitable for the effort.
<p>Thanks for playing,
<p>Rich Waters
<br>Lead Designer, EverQuest
</blockquote>
<p>In other words, folks, if you wait until the next patch, the spell will be easier to obtain. The quest will stay in game for those of us who enjoy playing with such stuff <i>{curls protectively around her fishing pole and her Misty Thicket Picnic}</i>, but for those who don't have a tradeskill junkie's patience with such quests, find enough patience to wait for the next patch. ;D
<p>I'm back to practicing my dual-wielding skills - foraging for tufts of dire wolf fur on one machine while tackling site updates on the other ... have fun with all the new recipes, everyone!
<p align="right">~DenMom</p> 2002-05-12 06:47:25 2003-06-12 02:39:49 2003-06-12 02:39:53 1 EQTC Editor Krazick

8 EQTC Editor Krazick Patch Day! It's another BIG day with regards to tradeskills, and it will be a while before updates hit the site and the dust settles. I'll make another update later today, once we have some solid information in place, but a few things to note in the meantime. 
<p><li>The initial writeup for the <a href="<!--server:x-->articles/article_page.php?article=q34&menustr=120010000000">Protection of the Cabbage quest</a> is up on the site, including the new earring reward. Nondruids who had been working on this quest should pay special note to the fact that the previous all/all earring is now druid-only. </li>
<li>Many new smithing recipes were put in today, as well as many new trivials. It WILL be mid-afternoon before even the first of these gets onto the site. It's even more important than ever that you READ before you post your questions and comments in the message boards, as we're going to be running a tight herd on the chaos caused by stampeding smiths. There are specific sticky topics set aside JUST for recipes and stats, and other threads set aside for questions. </li>
<li>Other quests, item stats, etc. have changed, and we'll get those updates on the site as able. </li>
<li>Rennet vendors are back in place. </li>
<li>Remember to watch your manners when posting on the message boards. A LOT of folks have been less-than-mannered lately, and have found themselves in the doghouse. The posting and conduct rules are there for a reason, and we are very actively enforcing them. This goes especially for those of you wanting to let off some steam. Even in the Primal Scream Forum, remember that the rules apply. Keep it family-rated, and remember NO personal attacks. We understand that when tradeskills change, folks tend to get a tad ... excited ... but this message board community really does NOT appreciate some of the foaming at the mouth we've seen lately. Such antics only distract us from making sure that data gets accurately reported, then recorded, onto the site. </li></ul>
<p><b>June 5, Addendum 1: </b>
<p>The following is a post from Rich Waters, one of the Lead Designers for EQ: 
<p><blockquote>If you are not a Druid and you've completed the PoTC quest, go and speak with Rebecca Cabbageleaf in Fungusgrove - She's more than happy to give you something you'll be able to use instead of Xanthe's Earring.
<p>If you're one of the few people who did the quest twice and lost an earring due to it being made lore, petition in game and a GM will reimburse you with the nine ingredients needed to make another earring after verifying your loss.
<p>If your Xanthe's Earring is out of charges, trade it in with Rebecca Cabbageleaf in Fungusgrove, and she'll give you one that has charges. When items that didn't have an effect are retroactively changed, it sometimes causes the "out of charges" bug. 
<p>To trade the earring in with Rebecca, give her your Xanthe's Earring and she'll give you an alternate kind of earring. Give her back the alternate earring, and she'll give you a fully charged Xanthe's earring back.
<p>Sorry for any inconvenience this has caused you, this should solve any difficulties anyone's had with the earring.
<p>Thanks,
<p>- Rich 
</blockquote> 2002-06-05 07:13:37 2005-03-04 04:32:31 2012-04-08 04:15:14 1 Ngreth Thergn
9 Niami Denmother I have several things to highlight today:
<p><blockquote>The new smithing recipes and trivials are slowly trickling in, and I have some requests to make, based on the first day\'s worth of data. Please be sure that when you\'re reporting on stats for new items, that you\'re including race/class/weight information. I know it takes a few extra moments to scribble it all down, but it really makes a difference on the completeness of information for the site. Please make sure you\'re clearly stating trivials - there\'s a difference between \"trivial 222\" and \"trivial <=222\". Make sure you\'re being fully clear if you know the <i>exact</i> trivial vs. it being trivial at that point or some point below. Please be sure that when you\'re reporting new trivials on old cultural items that you are explicitly stating whether you\'re working in racial chain or plate for things like dark elven and high elven armors. It may seem like a little thing, but when we\'re already dealing with normal, enchanted, and imbued/enchanted armor, I refuse to \"assume\" that I know which set you\'re talking about.
<p>That having been said, there is a lot of data already on the appropriate smithing pages. If you find a smithing page that does <i>not</i> include two trivial colums (old & new), then I have not yet processed any new information for that specific group of items. This may mean that nobody has submitted any new information, or it may just mean that I\'ve not reached that part of the huge pile of updates that have been dropped in my lap.
<p>Yes, I\'m aware that pretty much every smithing guide in the Learn Smithing section is now totally outdated. This situation isn\'t likely to change until new trivials are more fully nailed down and folks start submitting new guides based on that information.
<p>I\'ve managed to verifiy race changes to halfling cultural tailored armor, but folks are slow in reporting in whether other of the new cultural items that were added on May 5 have had stats changed based on yesterday\'s patch. Wood elves, especially, please check all those lovely tailored armors of yours, and report in if anything has changed with your armor. (I\'m hoping half elf was added to the sets.)
<p>Contrary to yesterday\'s patch message, enchanted clay is still not stacking. Whoops! 
<p>More updates have been done to the <a href=\"http://www.eqtraders.com/quests/potc_intro.htm\">PoTC quest writeup</a>, including the addition of the non-tradeskill spell-only version of the quest. It still needs a lot of fleshing out, but that\'s going to take more time than I currently have.
<p>The mailbox to which all my private EZBoard messages are sent is beyond overflowing with viruses, trojan horses, spam, unwanted trash as well as various stray emails from folks who need my attention. I\'m afraid to say that I\'m beyond behind responding to any real mail that might be lurking in that mailbox, and it\'s not likely to change any time in the near future. In some cases, I cannot respond as the people in question have not included any email address in their message (EZBoards doesn\'t include your email addy on private messages). Additionally, I\'m having problems with my ISP that I use for <i>the rest</i> of my email, and it\'s been timing out left, right, sideways and diagonally for the last several days. For the dozen or so of you offering to take over the fashion section, however, I\'m going to close down that section of the site. Due to a horde of problems, as well as system load, it\'s not feasible for this site to track every single new/old set of player-made armor and track two versions of the graphics for them (with and without Luclin models).
<p>Folks have started emailing moderators when they have problems registering an EZBoard account. Unfortunately, we don\'t own EZBoards, so it\'s rather hard for us to troubleshoot these. You\'ll want to report such problems in directly to the EZBoard <a href=\"http://pub121.ezboard.com/fezboardaccountproblemsfrm1\">Login/Support</a> Forum and see if they can help. (You don\'t need to be registered/logged in to post to that forum.)
<p>I\'ve developed zero tolerance for certain antics on the message boards. Please remember that the Primal Scream Forum, as is mentioned on the banner text when you enter that forum does not allow personal attacks (name-calling, slander, etc.), and yes, saying \"I hope you @#$ \'ing die\" is WELL beyond acceptable behavior and is subject to immediate banning. We also ask, rather clearly, that you \"keep it clean\". Unmasked swearing in subject lines, as well as swearing (however masked) <i>at specific people</i> are also not acceptable. For those that are unaware of the history of that forum, it was originally meant as a spot where people could rant and rave out their tradeskill frustrations after a horrible run of luck, etc., while still keeping it within the realms of polite public behavior. While we\'ve allowed some leeway on what\'s allowed in there, it is still not a place to come in and spew filth. There are plenty of other message boards in the world where you can spew that trash if you really need to, but we don\'t need it in our community.</blockquote> 2002-06-06 07:25:45 2002-11-03 07:25:45 2003-02-12 01:54:20 1 EQTC Editor Tobin Itharel
10 Niami Denmother Just a few quick updates:
<p>Cazic-Thule jewelcraft has been deciphered, and the first pieces have been successfully made. Recipes and stats are on the <a href=\"http://www.eqtraders.com/secrets/recipes_cazicthule.htm\">Cazic-Thule recipes page</a>.
<p>The dust is finally starting to slowly settle from the June 5 patch and all the changes to smithing trivials. It\'s still going to take a while to get it all updated, but we\'re getting there. For all of those asking on the various forums, as far as we know <i>only</i> smithing trivials were changed.
<p>There\'s another patch this Wednesday. Hopefully the rockhoppers and sambata that share a cave in Dawnshroud Peaks will find their way home again, as well as a few other spawn issues. :) We\'ll have more of an update Wednesday.
<p>We received the following suggestion on our Quests message board, and there\'s already been responses that it does help when having problems with quest NPCs:
<p><blockquote>If any NPC is not responding to direct text do this. Clear your target window and say the quest text. For some reason they will respond when you do NOT have them targeted. So just make sure you don\'t have a target at all by pressing the escape key.</blockquote>
<p>As an addendum to this, close your inventory window before you hail them, as this has been reported to be one issue with non-responsive NPCs. If that doesn\'t work, close your eyes, stand on one foot, bay at the moon and hit the ENTER key ... wait, sorry, that last bit is the Bristlebane in me. Try the non-targeted talk and the inventory closed if you\'re having problems with an NPC, and, as always, remember to research in advance to verify that you have the proper faction, proper text, etc. 
<p><b>Administrivia:</b> we\'re working on collecting all the information needed to have a comprehensive tradeskill database that will allow cross-referencing of trade supplies, sources (vendors, mob drops, etc.) and recipes. It\'s a huge undertaking, and it\'s going to take a lot of time to get it ready for public viewing. If you see requests in one of the forums asking for help collecting data, that\'s why, and the information we need the most is on the exotic stuff - tradeskill drops off mobs, player-made cultural items that are then used as ingredients for other recipes (i.e., adamantite chain jointing, and other such things) and so on. So, as you\'re tradeskilling and shopping, the data that you get from a right-click is likely exactly what we\'re looking for. Keep an eye on the various forums for a request for your tradeskill(s). Meanwhile, this half-blind hobbit is toddling off tomorrow for lasik eye surgery,and is supposed to be MIA from the boards and other eye-strain until sometime Wednesday (patch day). Wish me luck! 2002-06-10 07:30:21 2002-11-03 07:30:21 0

17 EQTC Editor Tobin Itharel Mischief and Mayhem <p>Fortunately, things are relatively quiet on the tradeskill front right now.
Discussion of the new EQ interface that is currently on Test can be found via <a href=\"http://pub126.ezboard.com/feqtraderscornerfrm64.showMessage?topicID=275.topic\" target=\"_new\">this
message board thread</a>. Some progress has been made at last on sorting out the
<a href=\"http://www.eqtraders.com/secrets/recipes_cazicthule.htm\">Cazic Thule
recipes</a>. As always, a lot of updates are going on behind the scenes on a
daily basis, especially in narrowing down smithing trivials, adding stats for
the newer tradeskill items, etc. A few weeks back, I also had to split apart the
cultural armor stats from the main armor stats page. This has caused quite a bit
of confusion, and it\'s currently not the most elegant or intuitive layout, but
it will have to do for the near future. For now, all smithed cultural armor
stats can be found a) via the nav buttons on the left-hand side of the <a href=\"http://www.eqtraders.com/secrets/recipes_smithing_armor_stats.htm\">main
armor stats page</a> and, b) via a link at the TOP of each cultural recipes page
for that culture\'s stats. I apologize for the kludgy feel of this, but it\'s
going to be a while before I can tackle nav issues.
<p>This brings me to the mischief and mayhem portion of this update. I\'ve been
dual-wielding computers for quite a while now, as it allows me to work on site
updates at the same time I am performing research in-game, wield both my
accounts at once to have easier access to tradeskill mules, etc. Unfortunately,
the setup I\'ve been using for the last couple of years is not ergonomic, and
hasn\'t been very good for my chronic back problems. We finally made arrangements
to have both my office and Ngreth\'s office redone, with setups that should make
them much more comfortable workplaces. We\'ve been planning this for a couple
months, and yesterday the movers arrived to box up everything in my office, so
the folks could come in today with the custom setup for my office. Ngreth\'s
office was to follow next Tuesday. Unfortunately, some wires were crossed
somewhere (I blame Bristlebane, may all his toe fur fall off!), and the
installers showed up today with <i>Ngreth\'s</i> office setup, not mine. They\'re
not even done building mine. Soooo ... Ngreth and two installers are busy
disassembling Ngreth\'s old office right now and packing it up, most of my office
possessions are taking over the guest room, my cats are frantic and hiding from
the chaos, and I ... am working off a card table set up in my almost-empty
office. I\'ll be working off this setup until Tuesday morning, at which time I
re-disassemble everything and pray there are no more surprises in store. (edit:
hubby\'s office is taking 2 days to complete, so I expect mine will as well ...
wheeeeee).
<p>{gibber}
<p>Needless to say, I\'ll likely get less accomplished than normal for the next
few days. 2002-06-26 12:00:00 0
18 EQTC Editor Tobin Itharel Unburying! <p>Well, it\'s a week later than I\'d originally planned, but my new home office
furniture is finally installed, and I\'ve got the 2 PCs and the laptop set back
up. It\'s going to take me quite a while to get the CDs, documentation, maps,
knicknacks, unpacked, sorted and put into their new spots, but I\'m already
enjoying the feeling of \"space\" that the new layout gives me. (The
extra storage space will also come in handy, as I\'m definitely a packrat!)
<p>Meanwhile, I\'m sure you folks are more interested in what\'s going on
tradeskill-wise, so here\'s a small update for you. Barren Flounder, that had
been chased into virtual extinction by the introduction of Timorous Tuna into
their spawning grounds back in November, have been seen once again in Erud\'s
Crossing on Test server. This is wonderful news for the \"good\" erudite
clerics, who have been unable to enjoy the use of faithstones that their other
healing brethren have been using. Hopefully it will be re-introduced onto the
live servers with the next patch. We\'re also hoping to see a few other item
tweaks next patch, such as to the stats of the Cazic Thule armor and weapons,
stackability of Tae Ew meat, etc.
<p>As time and oomph permit, I\'m going through all <a href=\"secrets/recipes_smithing_armor_stats.htm\">the
armor stats pages</a> to see what\'s missing for the older smithed armor sets. As
I\'m finding missing data, the relevant stats page is having question marks added
in the appropriate spots, and on the more major information, I\'m <a href=\"http://pub126.ezboard.com/feqtraderscornersmithing.showMessage?topicID=6540.topic\">whimpering
for help</a> on data that I can\'t find elsewhere. After I tackle all the armors
(I\'m about a third of the way through the cultural sets now), I\'ll tackle the
smithed weapons. Those of you with a solid player-made weapon collection are
more than welcome to compare what\'s on the weapon stats page with the
information on your weapons, and post with missing information in that same
message board thread.
<p>My thanks to Fallenhero for the new art at the top of this page. We try very
hard to keep the site fast-loading, without a lot of extra frufru, but it\'s
amazing how a couple tiny files make a difference. :)
<p>For the Americans amongst us, may you have a happy and <i>safe</i>
Independence Day tomorrow.</p> 2002-07-03 12:00:00 0
