103 Ngreth Thergn Ngreth's Guild Summit Summary <p>After finally receiving our invite, Niami decided to send the House Ogre instead
  of herself to the Guild Summit. With that you were already doomed to poor writing!
  But I will press on and do the best I can. I also did not bring a camera, so
  we will have to muddle on without pictures.</p>
<p>Being local, and having to work on Friday, I declined to show up at the Baseball
  Game, and instead came in for breakfast Saturday morning. Once there I shook
  a few hands, and then sat down to chat with a few guild leaders/representatives,
  two of them being leaders on the server I actually play on.</p>
<p>After Breakfast, The group was bussed to SOE (where since I drove, I missed
  the big group picture.. oh well) where we sat in the nice hot San Diego weather
  while John Smedley gave us an introduction to what we should expect for the
  day. One big revelation was this: Gates of Discord was intended to work with a
  level cap increase to be released on the 5th anniversary of Everquest. Because
  of this the zones were tuned for level 68 or 70, making it the WAY too difficult
  beast that we faced. Additionally, a developer that is no longer with SOE (no
  more than that was said about the developer, as I am sure they are legally
  required to not say anything more) decided to play with waaaaay high attack
  skill numbers on the mobs. Put these two together, and you got the near-impossible
  expansion that we got.</p>
<p>Now that said, they have tuned Gates of Discord down, and reduced the overly
  high attack skills of the mobs, so that it is much more possible than before,
  though the later zones are still raid oriented. So if you had a bad experience
  before, you should go try it out again. (The main part of the retuning went
  in two patches ago, though they are still doing some final tweaking.)</p>
<p>Another interesting piece of information that was given out was that the largest
  segment of EverQuest fans are level 30 to 50. They do NOT base this on just
  the number of characters at the level, but at the amount of playtime in those
  levels.</p>
<p>There was also talk about how BETA can be improved, and they are open to suggestions.
  They are planning on trying to invite more "uber guild" in total
  to help them with testing. These guilds would be Character Copied over in full.
  (At a dinner later in the evening, I found out that a guild was invited in
  whole, and copied, to help beta test Gates of Discord, but they decided they
  would rather raid on live server than help Beta test... so were not useful
  during the testing. This is a problem in general where testers go raid with
  their
  guild on live instead of testing as they have been invited... instead they
  just hang long enough to get "strats" for live release.) They may
  even bring back the "token" system that was used in PoP beta to help
  convince people to test.</p>
<p>During this chat they said that though marketing folks will be around to listen,
  they are NOT there to sell us anything. And I can say they did not make any
  attempt to push anything on us while we were there :) That is not to say there
  was not any marketing at all, it was voluntary. (I will explain this more soon.)</p>
<p>The biggest thing I want to bring from the initial conversation is this. The
  Developers themselves love the game, they want to make a fun game, and a game
  that you want to play. They play the game themselves, and want it to be fun.
  The developers pay includes royalties from the games, so they want it to sell.
  Though not directly in the conversation, it seems that for whatever reason
  the decision makers were not listening to the developers. This summit is to keep that from
  happening again. The developers will listen to us, and the decision makers
  will listen to the developers</p>
<p>Next we were taken on a tour of the three buildings that make up the SOE compound.
  We got to see a few of the servers that make up the game. Many of the servers
  were in an off site building, but a few were there. Each server is 30 dual
  pentium 4's with 2 gigs of ram. There are 48 servers, making for 1440 computers
  for just the server hardware. This does not include dev clusters, login servers,
  chat servers, databases ... so you can imagine the huge undertaking it is. There
  was some indirect information indicating they run Raid 5's, but raid 5's do
  not preclude disasters, just make them rarer and more recoverable :) If two
  drives fail at the same time (rare, but not statistically impossible) data
  loss can occur. FULL backups are made daily, so the worst case is a full days
  rewind.</p>
<p>At the end of the tour, they pointed out a room where they will be showing
  Omens of War and Epic 2.0 graphics. They said that during lunch we can go in
  and see if we wish. That was the extent of the marketing push. Of course many
  people wanted to see epic 2.0, so the room was crowded :)</p>
<p>After the tour, we settled down into 5 smaller groups to speak with the developers
  about our concerns. The following is what we spoke about, basically in the
  order in which I wrote it down. <strong>NONE of this is a promise that this
  will be done, this is just a listing of the discussions we had.</strong> I
  will mention when the developers gave ideas of what they would like to do,
  but of course all has to go through approvals and time before they will become
  reality.</p>
<ul>
  <li>There was a request for Group and Guild /corpse commands
    <ul>
      <li>The current system creates a "list" of people that have permission
        to drag your corpse. A few ideas go with this. They are thinking of adding
        group, guild, and raid as valid elements to the list. Another possibility
        will to add options that you can turn on with slash commands and in the
        options window. These options will allow you to turn on group, guild,
        and raid dragging as a switch, meaning that all elements in the group,
        raid, or guild will be able to drag your corpse until you turn off the
        switch. One other thought on this, to make the draggers life easier, would
        be to allow a "drag" command which locks the corpse to the person, no
        longer requiring them to spam the /corpse command to drag. This would
        also allow the dragger to drag a group of corpses easily</li>
    </ul>
  </li>
  <li>A request for RAID MOTD options in order to list items such as Main Assist,
    designated buffers, and such information.
    <ul>
      <li>Dev response: Basically looking into it, and liking the idea</li>
    </ul>
  </li>
  <li>There was a request for sounds to be sendable or activatable.
    <ul>
      <li>This one went a different direction and greatly expanded. The developers
        indicated that they were interested in adding a "filter" that you can
        customize to make sounds if you see certain words or phrases. This went
        on with
        ever expanding ideas from adding options to add sounds on tells, group, and raid
        chat to fully customizable context-sensitive filtered chat windows.
        The results of this conversation were not clear.</li>
    </ul>
  </li>
  <li>There was an Official statement about the rumor that certain amounts of
    AA's will be needed in order to gain levels when the level cap is increased.
    <ul>
      <li><strong><font color="#339999">The developers officially confirmed that
            this is a FALSE rumor. The new level caps will NOT be dependent on
            the
            player having certain amounts of AA points. Players can still advance
            without getting any AA points.</font></strong></li>
    </ul>
  </li>
  <li>In response to requests for a method to recover augments, and not have
    them destroyed...
    <ul>
      <li>The Developers indicated that it is in the works, they are still working
        on the balance and cost factor of it, but it is definitely planned. It
        may even be a trade skill item that allows it to be done. Nothing is
        set in stone.</li>
    </ul>
  </li>
  <li>There was a request for a guild bank.
    <ul>
      <li>They are looking into it, and it has a chance to go, but realistically
        the whole Guild code needs to be reworked. More on this later.</li>
    </ul>
  </li>
  <li>During this time I brought up that we want the appropriate developers to
    be given the time they need to fix the "old" trade skill issues, the main
    ones being Cultural Holes, and PoP drop rate.
    <ul>
      <li>Seeing neither Maddoc nor Absor were in the dev group I was working
        with, the developers I was with dutifully wrote it down :)</li>
    </ul>
  </li>
</ul>

<p>After this conversation we all had a cookout lunch. During this time I did
  speak with Maddoc, and put through that we want him to have time to fix the
  cultural and PoP issues :) So the info go the the correct person. I also decided to
  go hit the game room where they were showing off OoW graphics. The graphics
  for many of the new epic 2.0's were there, and even though the particle effects
  were not in, nor was the animation in yet, they were gorgeous (though I was
  not pleased with the looks of the Mage epic...)</p>
<p>After lunch, we had a meeting with a representative of the Customer Service
  team. The main thing they wanted to say is that they are introducing a new
  service for guilds. The introduced a guild dispute hotline. For certain issues,
  (only) a guild leader will be able to send mail to a mailbox and get priority
  assistance. This is a pilot program, and they will listen to feedback to make
  it better. Click on the image link to see the handout we were given.<br />
  <a href="../images/articles/GuildCSSmaller.jpg"><!--image_op:GuildCSThumb.jpg..77..100..0--></a><br />
  The most common thread of what people wanted was a way for up to 2 people other
  than the guild leader to also have permission to send mail, so that the guild
  leader is not forced with another task, or to ALWAYS be on. My handwriting
  on the page is for what additional information you can include to help make
  the letter sent more useful.</p>
<p>Each server has a dedicate GM from 2-11pm. The rest of the time, there is
  a pool of GM's that roam servers (this same pool is around during the dedicated
  time to help with large loads)</p>
<p>Be liberal with your use of /report. /report records the line of text right
  above the chat input line, and the 19 lines above this. This means you can
  scroll back to get the text you want. It will record those 19 lines even if
  they are not visible. One thing they were not clear about (because they were
  not sure) is it MAY record those 20 lines in ALL open chat windows. If you
  want proof of people being in an area. Do /who and then /report the /who results.
  This will be taken as proof while screen shots will not be taken as proof.
  SO sometimes you do have to anticipate problems :/</p>
<p>One thing they said was, if all else fails, and it is the last few seconds,
  loot the item. It is **NOT** likely that the item will be moved to the correct
  person. It will be very situational. But if the item is allowed to rot on a
  corpse, it absolutely will not be reimbursed. There is no log of items on
  mob corpses, there is a log of items looted. The customer service personnel
  have no way to tell what was on a corpse, so will not reimburse from it. *IF*
  you can show some proof that the person was around for the encounter (/report!)
  and that they were not able to loot for a game reason (Link dead is not a
  game reason), they *MAY* "move" the item (more like delete from one inventory
  and add to the other). So the basics is this, as a last resort, and a last
  resort only, do not let an item rot on a mob corpse, loot the item and hope
  that the planets are aligned correctly and you can get the item moved. Do not
  expect this to allow you to loot items for a person not around. They really
  need proof that the person was there for that particular encounter, and that
  SOE game issues prevented the person from looting (again, Link Death is NOT
  an SOE issue in normal situations... normally it is an ISP issue, and does
  not count)</p>
<p>The Guide program will be changed from them actively answering petitions,
  to them being an "event' troupe. They will go around running events on the
  server, making it more alive and dynamic.</p>
<p>After this conversation, developers were brought in again to have more conversations,
  this one more focused on what we want to see in the future, than what we want
  fixed.</p>
<ul>
  <li>Guild Tribute will cost 2/3 of the individual tribute, PER PERSON... so
    if an ability costs 60 tribute per 10 minutes for the individual, it will
    cost 40 tribute per 10 minutes per person ONLINE in the guild at the time.
    Some will stack, some will take "best" depending on the buff given.</li>
  <li>This brought up a whole conversation about guilds, and wanting more customizable
    guild rankings. The developers we spoke to seemed open to it, but indicated
    that it will probably take a whole guild system rewrite, and that they WANT
    to
    do this. It will just take prioritizing.</li>
  <li>There was a request to do something about stuns and mezs and similar things
    being all or nothing. The request was for a way to have these be partial,
    like have the attack ability be reduced in response to a partial. The developers
    did not seem very receptive to this, but they did not say no either.</li>
  <li>There was a request to have it possible to have AA's refunded, or just
    removed. The developers were very noncommittal to this.</li>
  <li>One side dev comment was that they will work really hard to make sure that
    future raid sizes are set to max 54 and not have the max changed around to
    more or less so that guilds can predict better.</li>
  <li>For epic 2.0 the final battle WILL be a raid (balanced to 54 people) If
    the raid succeeds at this step, you WILL receive the item needed at this
    step. It will not be chance as many epic 1.0's were.</li>
  <li>There may be "partial" epics (1.5) for more casual people to reach, without
    having to do the full final raid.</li>
  <li>Typical epic documents are 20-30 pages long. These will be epic.</li>
  <li>Epic 2.0s are being looked at carefully to ensure that there are of similar
    difficulty.</li>
  <li>There was a suggestion for more consumables for trade skills other than
    baking, brewing, and alchemy. The idea is for items with charges or whatever,
    for
    all trade skills, for a continual source of income for trade skills</li>
  <li>New Character models for the new graphics engine are in the works, but
    are far off from being even previewed, much less implemented.</li>
  <li>Except for specific accepted events, events will be tuned to last 2 hours
    on average, as the target length.</li>
  <li>There was a request to make some of the Kunark, and Velious "boss" mobs
    or "uber" mobs spawn more often than once a week.</li>
  <li>It was revealed that point expenditure for GoD AA was tuned to Plane of
    Fire experience gain rate.</li>
  <li>They will consider the "Flowing Thought" (mana regen) cap.</li>
  <li>There is a work in progress already to make the titles available in game
    choose able by the user. You will be able to choose from titles that you
    are eligible for. They will be adding titles for race and trade skills. There
    MAY be some combination titles, but they have not committed to those.</li>
  <li>There was in idea to add a "raid vendor" at the end of raid adventures
    and expeditions to allow for "higher" raid only prizes not available from
    the more public vendors.</li>
  <li>It was revealed that LDoN raids are only 30 points because the loot drops
    given during the raid were also considered part of the reward.</li>
  <li>I forwarded the idea that we want more solstice earring, and shawl type
     recipes and quests... it was given hearty approval by the players in the
    same group :)</li>
  <li>Another idea was forwarded (not by me) to have certain recipes be "loot".
    This would mean you have to earn the loot to make the item.</li>
</ul>
<p>After this last meeting we went to dinner, where we took over a room at a
  club/restaurant and mingled with each other and the developers. Maddoc even
  chose to sit next to me and put up with the firing line :) During this dinner
  we
  were given a document of initial plans. CLick on the image bellow to see it.<br />
  <a href="../images/articles/OfficialSummitSummarySmaller.jpg"><!--image_op:OfficialSummitSummaryThumb.jpg..77..100..0--></a><br />
  One thing to note.  The dev responsible for fixing the collision problems,
  is still working on it, and will continue to work on it. These plans will be
  assigned to other developers :)</p>
<p>All in all I got the idea that the developers really do want to make a game
  we want to play, so please, don't accuse the developers of ignoring the players,
  it never
  was them that was doing so!</p>
<p> </p> 2004-06-08 01:33:31 2004-06-10 02:13:40 2004-06-10 02:04:00 0 Niami Denmother

108 Krazick DB Master Database Turns **ONE** today <h3>This day in History</h3>
<p>There are websites out there that will give you some historical notes about what happened on any particular day of the year. And July 21 is a interesting day... One site tells me that on July 21 there were some interesting milestones occurred:</p>

<ul>
<li>1904 (100 years ago) Camille Jenatzy sets world auto speed record at 65.79 MPH</li>
<li>1954 (50 years ago) At Geneva, France agrees to independence of North & South Vietnam</li>
<li>1969 (35 years ago) Neil Armstrong steps on the Moon</li>
<li>1984 (20 years ago) 1st documented case of a robot killing a human in US (Is Will Smith onto something?)</li>
</ul>

<p>[Note there are lots more, I just selected a few]</p>

<p>So why do I bring this up today? It is simple, there is another milestone to add to the list, but it most likely will never be on par with any of these events...</p>

<p>The EQ Traders Database turns ONE year old today. That's right, it was on July 21, 2003 that Niami & Ngreth released the database to all you EQ Tradeskill Fanatics. To give you an idea of where we were, and where we are now I have a few statistics:</p>

<ul>
<li>12 Tables to properly track all of the Items, Mobs, Recipes, Sources, and Zones</li>
<li>1 Table for the 179 Quest Articles</li>
<li>1 Table for the 254 Guide Articles</li>
<li>1 Table for the 97 News Articles</li>
</ul>

<h3>Record Count:</h3>
<ul>
<li>Recipes</li>
<ul>
<li>2003 > 6,000</li>
<li>2004 = 8,879 (577 KB Space)</li>
</ul>

<li>Recipe Supporting Tables</li>
<ul>
<li>2004 = 59,690 Records from 5 Tables (1,843.3 KB Space)</li>
</ul>
<li>Items</li>
<ul>
<li>2003 > 8,000</li>
<li>2004 = 11,159 (1,900 KB Space)</li>
</ul>
<li>Mobs</li>
<ul>
<li>2003 > 2,500</li>
<li>2004 = 2,930 (236.7 KB Space)</li>
</ul>
<li>Sources</li>
<ul>
<li>2003 about 2,000</li>
<li>2004 = 2,543 (239.5 KB Space)</li>
</ul>
<li>Source Supporting Tables</li>
<ul>
<li>2004 = 15,554 Records from 2 Tables (689 KB Space)</li>
</ul>
<li>Zones</li>
<ul>
<li>2004 = 204 (14.7 KB Space)</li>
</ul>

<li>TOTAL Records: 101,190 (5,467 KB or 5.5 MB of Space)</li>
<li>TOTAL Articles: 530 (2,600 KB or 2.6 MB of Space)</li>
</ul> 2004-07-21 06:18:22 2004-07-21 07:44:24 2004-10-06 03:35:09 1 Niami Denmother

110 Ngreth Thergn Racknine performing a network upgrade. I got the following note from RackNine.
<blockquote><p>From September 8th through 11th RackNine will be making changes to its network architecture and short outages may affect portions of the network while traffic is re-routed to increase capacity. During this period trouble ticket and email support may be inaccessible and I?d recommend calling toll-free for any inquiries.</p>

256 Coldain Prayer Shawl 2.0 #2 - Will it Live? <h4>Will it Live? </h4>
<p>This is the 2nd task in the Coldain Shawl 2.0 series. You must have previously completed '<a href="<!--server:x-->articles/article_page.php?article=q255&menustr=120000000000">Still Hungry</a>' and have a raw pottery skill of 300 to request this task.</p>
 
<p>Quest NPC: Chamberlain Thoridain, Brell's Temple</p>
 
<h4>Task Steps:</h4>
<ul>
<li>Speak with Foreman Gribblebitz ? Foundation</li>
<li>Find some fresh clay in the foundation - Foundation</li>
<li>Retrieve some clay from a clay golem - Foundation</li>
<li>Loot 1 Cliknar Claimed Clay Sample from any cliknar - Foundation</li>
<li>Collect some Clay of Cosgrove - Brell's Temple (1) </li>
<li>Collect some Purest Water - Brell's Temple (5) </li>
<li>Create 1 Unfired Clay Statue using tradeskills - Brell's Temple</li>
<li>Create 1 Unfired Clay Statue using tradeskills - Brell's Temple</li>
<li>Create 1 Unfired Clay Statue using tradeskills - Brell's Temple</li>
<li>Create 1 Unfired Clay Statue using tradeskills - Brell's Temple</li>
<li>Create 1 Unfired Clay Statue using tradeskills - Brell's Temple</li>
<li>Deliver 1 Clay Statue to Chamberlain Thoridain - Brell's Temple</li>
<li>Deliver 1 Clay Statue to Chamberlain Thoridain - Brell's Temple</li>
<li>Deliver 1 Clay Statue to Chamberlain Thoridain - Brell's Temple</li>
<li>Deliver 1 Clay Statue to Chamberlain Thoridain - Brell's Temple</li>
<li>Deliver 1 Clay Statue to Chamberlain Thoridain - Brell's Temple</li>
<li>Wear your Blessed Underfoot Prayer Shawl and speak with Chamberlain Thoridatin - Brell's Temple</li>

<h4>Details:</h4>
<p>Start by hailing Chamberlain Thoridain after having received the Blessed Underfoot Prayer Shawl.</p>
 
<p>You say, 'Hail, Chamberlain Thoridain'</p>
<p>Chamberlain Thoridain says 'You have done well on your first trial but so far there has been no reaction from Brell. While this is unexpected, we should continue if we hope to accomplish anything. Are you ready to [begin] the second trial?'</p>
<p>You say, 'begin'</p>
<p>You have been assigned the task 'Will it Live?'.</p>
<p>Chamberlain Thoridain says 'Very well. This trial will have you working with various types of Cosgrove Clay to create some simple statues. We will even see if you can bring life to them. I have given you a tool you will need during part of the quest. If you loose it you can ask me for another [tool], but please be careful, it takes time to make each tool. Good luck!'</p>
 
<p>Chamberlain Thoridain will give you a Pure Water collecting tool. No stats, goes in primary.</p>
 
<p>You are going to need to travel to the Foundation. In the farm not far from the zone in is Foreman Gribblebitz.</p>
 
<p>You say, 'Hail, Foreman Gribblebitz'</p>
<p>Your task 'Will it Live?' has been updated.</p>
<p>Foreman Gribblebitz says 'What? Oh, you are one of them. And Thoridain sent you? Well. Oh Clay. Yes, yes, here you go.'</p>
 
<p>This will get you the Gribblebitz clay sample. Next you will want to go ahead and ask him about the clay as well.</p>
 
<p>You say, 'what clay'</p>
<p>Foreman Gribblebitz says 'Oh no! You have been destroying the golems for their clay? No! That will not do! They are important! Here, take this sample tool and get your clay sample that way. What is wrong with all of you people? The first thing you want to do is destroy! If you have not been destroying them, I apologize for my assumptions, but you see what I am dealing with all of the time!'</p>
 
<p>He will give you a clay sampling device. This device will allow you to retrieve the sample from a clay golem. While next to a clay golem, you can use the device, be warned they will attack as well as any other mobs around them. This will give you the golem clay sample.</p>
 
<p>If you run around the west side of Foundation, over the small little pits, eventually you will get one that pops an item onto your cursor. This is the Foundation clay sample.</p>
 
<p>Also over on the west area of Foundation you will find plenty of cliknar mobs. Simply kill them until you get one to drop a cliknar claimed clay sample and loot it.</p>
 
<p>The pure water collection tool requires to be sterilized before it can be used each time. To do this, you combine the Pure water collection tool with a vodka in a kiln. This creates a Sterilized Pure Water Collecting Tool. Also, you will need to bring idol sketches, sculpting tools, and high quality firing sheets with you to Brell's Temple. The combines for the statues must be done on the pottery wheel and kiln located in Brell's Temple. They are in the main room that Brell paces around on the west side of the room.</p>
 
<p>From that central room, you will need to clear the mobs in the first room to the west of Brell's room. There is 1 roamer and 4 static spawns. Once all 4 static spawns are dead, simply walk up to the center area, and the clay of cosgrove should appear on your cursor. With all 5 clay samples you will need to clear to the east of the central room. There are 4 static spawns in this room as well. When all are dead, simply walk into the water fountain/pool in the middle of the room with a sterilized pure water collection tool. You will get a vial of purest water and the collection tool back. Run back to the kiln and resterilize your tool and run back. Repeat this until you have all 5 vials of the purest water. Now go over to the pottery wheel in the main central room. Combine an idol sketch + scultping tools + a vial of purest water with each of the 5 clay samples. You will craft 5 unfired clay statues. Next simply fire them in Brell's Temple in the kiln with a high quality firing sheet. Once you have fired all 5 statues, you turn them in to Chamberlain Thoridain. Once you have turned in all 5, simply put on your Blessed Underfoot Prayer Shawl and hail Chamberlain Thoridain again then turn it in to him.</p>
 
<p>If you were to fail one of the combines on the statues, you can simply hail Chamberlain Thoridain and he will give you the replacements so you do not have to recollect them from mobs.</p>
 
<p>You say, 'Hail, Chamberlain Thoridain'</p>
<p>Chamberlain Thoridain says 'Great. Give me your Blessed Underfoot Prayer Shawl, and I will give you your next shawl.'</p>
<p>Your task 'Will it Live?' has been updated.</p>
<p>Your task 'Will it Live?' has been updated.</p>
<p>You have expanded your knowledge of the clay of cosgrove.</p>
<p>You gain experience!!</p>
<p>Chamberlain Thoridain says 'Yes, you have done very well. Not only did you learn that the clay that comes to Brell's Temple is special, you also offered a prayer to Brell just in the act of creating in his presence. Here is your new shawl.'</p>
 
<p>At this point you will receive the <!--item_linkedname:37489-->.</p>
 
<p>You say, 'Hail, Chamberlain Thoridain'</p>
<p>Chamberlain Thoridain says 'While your skills with the Clay of Cosgrove were impressive, it has not moved the Creator. I must admit I have some doubts as to the chances of success but even so, we must try. Are you [willing] to test your skills in the third trial?'</p>
<p>You say, 'willing'</p>
<p>You have been assigned the task 'Sewing it Forward'.</p>
 
<p>This begins the 3rd task in the series '<a href="<!--server:x-->articles/article_page.php?article=q257&menustr=120000000000">Sewing it Forward</a>'</p> XXX 2011-02-26 08:03:47 2011-02-24 09:16:08 EQTC Editor Aanuvane 0 0 2011-02-26 08:01:01 EQTC Editor Aanuvane

125 CleavingWarlord Cleaving the Warlord - A Poem by Nherko E. Llafsnot <p>
If ye have bested Tallon, <br />
 and Vallon, too (or not?), <br />
 then get thee down to Eriak, <br />
 and there ask him, "What blood?" 
</p>
<p>
He'll draw his blade and cut himself, <br />
 and spill for you his own, <br />
 now take this vial, mount your steed, <br />
 and ride to Saryrn's zone. 
</p>
<p>
Find you there her constructs, <br />
 of which there are four breeds, <br />
 Insanity Fangs they'll drop for you-- <br />
 these stasify your needs. 
</p>
<p>
Into the barrel--fangs and blood, <br />
 celestial solvent, too, <br />
 to get one of the tempers, <br />
 proceed you now to brew. 
</p>
<p>
Now off to Valor go with haste, <br />
 and ride up to the swamp, <br />
 o'er everything that spawns up there, <br />
 shall you proceed to romp. 
</p>
<p>
Valorium shards, no drop, take these! <br />
 but whatever you do, <br />
 be sure the one that takes 'em, <br />
 is someone who can brew. 
</p>
<p>
Then ride again to Knowledge, <br />
 and then much like before, <br />
 except without the blood, of course, <br />
 brew up one temper more. 
</p>
<p>
Now head on back to Tactics, <br />
 and take a bunch of friends, <br />
 for in its depths drops ore with which, <br />
 this Zek-Bane quest will end. 
</p>
<p>
Tagrin Maldric spawns down there, <br />
 a troll both big and bad, <br />
 kill him there--but not too fast! <br />
 because you'll need his adds. 
</p>
<p>
Smiths will loot his guardians, <br />
 these flying swords--Decorins, <br />
 then (with water) find a forge, <br />
 to put Decorin ore in. 
</p>
<p>
Drunder's Steel--that's the thing, <br />
 with which you'll end this trial-- <br />
 into the forge with proper molds, <br />
 and aforebrewed blue vial. 
</p>
<p>
Almost done! It's good so far, <br />
 but there is more to do! <br />
 forge it now with your black vial, <br />
 and so your quest concludes. 
</p>
<p>
<i>The above member-written poem beautifully provides the "spoilers" for unraveling the mystery of the Zek-bane weapons quest. The <a href="<!--server:x-->articles/article_page.php?article=q24&menustr=120055000000">quest writeup</a>, is described.</i>
</p> XXX 2003-06-10 03:00:32 2003-06-10 03:00:32 EQTC Editor Krazick 0 0 2003-06-10 02:59:07 EQTC Editor Krazick

255 CPS20_1 Coldain Prayer Shawl 2.0 #1 - Still Hungry <h4>Still Hungry </h4>
<p>This is the first quest in the Coldain Shawl 2.0 series. To request this task you must have your Blessed Coldain Prayer Shawl and a raw skill of 300 in baking. A walkthrough of the Velious era prayer shawl quest can be found <b><a href="<!--server:x-->articles/article_page.php?article=q262&menustr=120000000000">here</b></a>.</P>
 
<p>Quest NPC: Chamberlain Thoridain, Brell's Temple</p>
 
<h4>Task steps:</h4>
<ul>
<li>Speak with Dorrvix - Brell's Rest</li>
<li>Create 1 Brell's Bounty Steamed Steaks using tradeskills - ALL</li>

<li>Deliver 1 Brell's Bounty Steamed Steaks to Dorrvix - Brell's Rest</li>

<li>Speak with Talbot Roaringhead - The Cooling Chambers</li>

<li>Create 1 Divine Snow Griffin Souffle using tradeskills - ALL</li>

<li>Deliver 1 Divine Snow Griffin Souffle to Talbot Roaringhead - The Cooling Chambers</li>

<li>Deliver 1 Divine Snow Griffin Souffle to Upper Foreman - The Cooling Chambers</li>

<li>Deliver 1 Divine Snow Griffin Souffle to Middle Forman - The Cooling Chambers</li>

<li>Deliver 1 Divine Snow Griffin Souffle to Lower Foreman - The Cooling Chambers</li>

<li>Speak with Yolgund Murkwader - The Underquarry</li>

<li>Create 1 Ale Marinated Cliknar Claws using tradeskills - ALL</li>

<li>Deliver 1 Ale Marinated Cliknar Claws to Yolgund Murkwader - The Underquarry</li>

<li>Speak with Turuff the Warrior - Kernagir, the Shining City</li>

<li>Create 1 Turuff's Favorite Meat using tradeskills - ALL</li>

<li>Deliver 1 Turuff's Favorite Meat to Turuff the Warrior - Kernagir, the Shining City</li>

<li>Speak with Master Alchemist Vakros - Brell's Temple</li>

<li>Create 1 Clockwork Stew using tradeskills - ALL</li>

<li>Deliver 1 Clockwork Stew to Master Alchemist Vakros - Brell's Temple</li>

<li>Wear your Blessed Coldain Prayer Shawl and speak to Chamberlain Thoridain - Brell's Temple</li>

<li>Deliver your Blessed Coldain Prayer Shawl to Chamberlain Thoridain - Brell's Temple</li>
</ul>

 
<h4>Combines:</h4>

<h4>Details:</h4>
<p>Upon zoning into Brell's Temple with your prayer shawl, you receive an emote.</p>
 
<p>"Chamberlain Thoridain says 'I sense a sacred relic of Brell on your person. If you would like to know more about this relic, come speak to me.'"</p>
 
<p>Chamblerlain Thoridain is located in the central room near Brell Serilis.</p>
<p>Hailing him starts the following dialogue.</p>
 
<p>You say, 'Hail, Chamberlain Thoridain'</p>
<p>Chamberlain Thoridain says 'Greetings upworlder, and welcome to the Temple of Brell. As soon as you entered the temple I could sense the energy of a sacred relic, though I am unable to determine which one. Would you be willing to [show] me the relic you possess?'</p>
<p>You say, 'show'</p>
<p>Chamberlain Thoridain says 'A Blessed Coldain Prayer Shawl! That brings back memories of my life in Thurgadin. Many ages ago, I served Brell there as a priest, much as I do now in His temple. The Thoridain family was responsiblefor testing those aspiring to the highest ranks of the shawl. Very few reached that point, and almost none ever attained what you now hold in your hands. To have earned such a relic of Brell is unheard of for one who is not a [Coldain].'</P>
<p>You say, 'coldain'</p>
<p>Chamberlain Thoridain says 'We consider ourselves to be His most devoted servants. In the time I have spent here, many new wonders were created. My understanding of the will of Brell expanded and was able to realize how much more we were capable of honoring our creator. With this new insight, I was inspired to devise a new series of trials for the devoted. Those who prove their worth would be rewarded new, more powerful shawls as symbols of their increasing [devotion to Brell].'</p>
<p>You say, 'devotion to brell'</p>
<p>Chamberlain Thoridain looks pained and says 'Despite our new devotion to Brell, something changed recently and he no longer speaks to us. He is consumed entirely with the creation of something and never leaves the workshop anymore. Perhaps we could help each other here. If you were willing to undertake the new trials showing your devotion, it might turn his attention to you, and in turn you would receive a much improved shawl for each trial you pass. Would you like to begin the first [trial]?'</p>
<p>You say, 'trial'</p>
<p>You have been assigned the task 'Still Hungry'.</p>
<p>Chamberlain Thoridain says 'Excellent! Although we are spirits and no longer require food, we still remember the wonderful taste. There are several whom I would like you to visit. Find out what food they would most like to have and prepare it for them. Although this may seem pointless, the effect on their spirits will be tremendous. Hopefully such an act of goodwill toward His followers will not go unnoticed.'</p>
 
<p>The first NPC is Dorrvix. Dorrvix is located in the gnoll camp in Brell's Rest.</p>
 
<p>You say, 'Hail, Dorrvix'</p>
<p>Your task 'Still Hungry' has been updated.</p>
<p>Dorrvix says 'You want know what Dorrvix want? Dorrvix want food. Dorrvix want Brell's [Bounty] [cooked] right way.'</p>
<p>You say, 'bounty'</p>
<p>Dorrvix says 'To make good cooked Brell's Bounty you need good Brell's Bounty, sauces, and spices. Don't forget steam best way to cook.'</p>
<p>You say, 'cooked'</P>
<p>Dorrvix says 'Yes. [Steam] only way. Other way cook too much.'</p>
<p>You say, 'steam'</p>
<p>Dorrvix says 'Dorrvix no know. You find steam. Maybe stick head in lava!'</p>
 
<p>Brell's Bounty are common ground spawns all throughout Brell's Rest and Cooling Chambers as well as can be foraged in the UF expansion. To prepare the brell's bounty you need to combine it in a mixing bowl with a water flask. The steam he speaks of is a drop from the elemenals in Brell's Rest, Essence of Steam. It is flagged as a quest item and used in tradeskills and is tradeable. Make the brell's bounty steam steaks in an oven/spit and hand it in to Dorrvix. Upon handing the item in to Dorrvix, you get the task to update and 
Dorrvix says 'Good good! Look good! Dorrvix eat. You go away now.'</p>
 
<p>Next you need to go to Cooling Chambers and speak with Talbot Roaringhead. Talbot is located in the 2nd room of dwarves.</p>
 
<p>You say, 'Hail, Talbot Roaringhead'</p>
<p>Your task 'Still Hungry' has been updated.</p>
<p>Talbot Roaringhead says 'Chamberlain Thoridain sent you to me to ask what I desire? That man deservers your respect, he is a great soul. Be sure you always speak to him with respect and speak of him well. What I desire will not be the easiest thing for you to get, it will even require that you go back to my homeland to retrieve a particular [egg].'</p>
<p>You say, 'egg'</p>
<p>Talbot Roaringhead says 'Yes. I long for the taste of snow griffon eggs. I know it is asking much of you, but it would really raise my spirits. If you will take on this task, I have a particular way to [cook] this that would be ideal and has never been done before.'</p>
<p>You say, 'cook'</p>
<p>Talbot Roaringhead says 'Take a single snow griffon egg and mix it with spices, neutralized goo acid and caveflower pollen. The neutralized acid will help the frothiness of the egg, and give a slight salt taste. The pollen will give a faint hint of honey to the overall dish. You should be able to find the neutralized acid and caveflower pollen within the cooling chamber.'</p>
 
<p>Snow griffin eggs if you recall were used in the first coldain shawl series and are an uncommon drop from the snow griffins that roam around the Eastern Wastes. These eggs are no drop. The caveflower pollen is a no drop, lore ground spawn near the zone in of cooling chambers. It is under a light producing flower at the bottom of the ramp that leads back out to Brell's Rest. It is not a very long respawn timer and if you bring a spit with you, along with the eggs and spices you can pick a few of them up while hunting the goos near the zone in for the acid. The neutralizing goo acid is an uncommon to rare drop from any goo model in the zone it is tradeable. Upon handing one of the divine snow griffin souffles in to Talbot, you receive the following message.</p>
 
<p>Talbot Roaringhead says 'Oh my. That is most excellent. I must commend you on a job well done. It is so well executed that I insist you share this with my foremen. I know that may not have been part of the original deal and may inconvenience you, but I truly insist.'</p>
 
<p>You now must deliver a souffle to each of the 3 foreman located in the cooling chambers. Simply head down the 2 paths and locate the 3 foreman. South path takes you to the upper foreman and deeper in will be the lower foreman by the lake. The middle foreman is down the east path from Talbot.</p>
<p>Once you hand all 3 in you are now ready to move on to the Underquarry and find Yolgund Murkwader.</p>
 
<p>You say, 'Hail, Yolgund Murkwader'</p>
<p>Your task 'Still Hungry' has been updated.</p>
<p>Yolgund Murkwader says 'So. The uppity Chamberlain Thordain sent ya to find what I desire. I desire a bit o' a break. Yes, I do enjoy the work, but I still need a break. I do nae forsee that happening, so perhaps I can kill two bugs with one weapon, and ye be my weapon. I desire ale marinated [cliknar] claws.'</p>
<p>You say, 'cliknar'</p>
<p>Yolgund Murkwader says 'The cliknar have turned into a scourge upon the underfoot. While I have never tasted their meat, I am willing to try it for the fact that you will need to kill some to make it. Take 3 claws, and marinate them in double brewed double stout dwarven ale and spices.'</p>
 
<p>Head into the southern stonequarry and then east into the silver mines of the Underquarry and you will find the cliknar. The models that stand up right with 4 arms have the chance to drop the intact cliknar claws, tradeable item. Then you need to brew or get a bottle of 2x brewed 2x stout dwarven ale. The easiest place I found was to go to Crescent Reach on the main floor as all the components are sold by vendors there to make the ale. Combine 3 of the claws with 1 of the ales and some spices in an oven or spit and return to the Underquarry and hand it in to Yolgund.</p>
 
<p>Your task 'Still Hungry' has been updated.</p>
<p>Yolgund Murkwader says 'Thank you. I will try this later. While it does not look appetizing, it does smell rather good.'</p>
 
<p>The next step is to find Turuff the Warrior in Kernagir, the Shining City. From the zone in you head NW to the first building and inside you go around the corner and will find a circle of about 10-12 NPCs. Turuff is a kobold standing by a pillar facing into the circle.</p>
 
<p>You say, 'Hail, Turuff the Warrior'</p>
<p>Your task 'Still Hungry' has been updated.</p>
<p>Turuff the Warrior says 'Turuff desire good [meat].'</p>
<p>You say, 'meat'</p>
<p>Turuff the Warrior says 'Turuff smart. Turuff know you know what best meat is and Turuff no need to tell you. You no trick Turuff. You know [gravy] as well.'</p>
<p>You say, 'gravy'</p>
<p>Turuff the Warrior says 'Yes. The gravy is good. Use much gravy. Be sure you chop meat too.'</p>
<p>The meat he desires is horse meat. You can find horse meat in PoR zones, Theater of Blood or Elddar Forest. You will need to grill the horse meat, combine in a mixing bowl, horse meat with a grilling sauce. The gravy he is referring to is brown gravy. This is made from vendor sold components, again I recommend Crescent Reach as it has all the components in the same zone. The gravy is made in an oven or spit and then you combine the grilled horse meat with 2 brown gravy and to chop it, you use a filleting knife. This is a crafted tool that is returned on success. Return to Kernagir and hand the Turuff's Favorite Meat back into Turuff.</p>
 
<p>Your task 'Still Hungry' has been updated.</p>
<p>Turuff the Warrior says 'See Turuff told you Turruf smart. Turuff find good person to make Turuff favorite food.'</p>
 
<p>Now you must go to Brell's Temple and in the central hub area where Brell Serilis paces you will find Master Alchemist Vakros.</p>
 
<p>You say, 'Hail, Master Alchemist Vakros'</p>
<p>Your task 'Still Hungry' has been updated.</p>
<p>Master Alchemist Vakros says 'Hello hello. Desire. But desire is not logical. But I can work with it anyway. I know what I desire. I desire a [Geerlok hypermodulating endospaning exotool].'</p>
<p>You say, 'Geerlok hypermodulating endospaning exotool'</p>
<p>Master Alchemist Vakros says 'Oh. You want to know what food I desire? How disappointing. Could you instead get me an [Ambleshift augmenting automator]?'</p>
<p>You say, 'ambleshift augmenting automator?'
Master Alchemist Vakros says 'Ok. Just food. I know. [Clockwork Stew].'</p>
<p>You say, 'clockwork stew'</p>
<p>Master Alchemist Vakros says 'You don't know how to make it? Well. You need to get organic clockwork oil, and then cook a clockwork balance gear in with grilled minotaur meat and vegetables in a pot. Are you sure you can handle that? Wait. Don't answer. You obviously do not have the skills. I won't count on getting it. Why did you even ask?'</p>
 
<p>Now you need to go back to Kernagir, the Shining City and kill any clockwork models throughout the zone to get the drops, organic clockwork oil and clockwork balance gear, both are tradeable. Minotaur meat can be found by killing minotaurs anywhere in Norrath, I recommend some place like Dragonscale Hills as it is fairly common there and tradeable. Combine the items together in an oven or spit and return to Brell's Temple to Vakros.</p>
 
<p>Your task 'Still Hungry' has been updated.</p>
<p>Master Alchemist Vakros says 'See. I told you you could do it. One should never doubt oneself. Thank you, I am sure I will enjoy eating this.'</p>
 
<p>The next step in the task is to equip your Blessed Coldain Prayer Shawl and hail Chamberlain Thoridain who is located in the same room as Vakros. </p>
 
<p>You say, 'Hail, Chamberlain Thoridain'</p>
<p>Chamberlain Thoridain says 'Great. Give me your Blessed Coldain Prayer Shawl, and I will give you your next shawl.'</p>
<p>Your task 'Still Hungry' has been updated.</p>
 
<p>After you hail Chamberlain Thoridain you hand your blessed coldain prayer shawl in to him.</p>
 
<p>Your task 'Still Hungry' has been updated.</p>
<p>You have taken the first step in your path.</p>
<p>You have gained 5 ability points! You now have 7 ability points.
You gain experience!!</p>
<p>Chamberlain Thoridain says 'Yes, you have done very well. Here is your new shawl with any augments you may have had.'</p>
 
<p>Completing this task I gained 5 aa and received the <!--item_linkedname:37488-->.</p>
 
<p>You say, 'Hail, Chamberlain Thoridain'</p>
<p>Chamberlain Thoridain says 'You have done well on your first trial but so far there has been no reaction from Brell. While this is unexpected, we should continue if we hope to accomplish anything. Are you ready to [begin] the second trial?'</p>
<p>You say, 'begin'</p>
<p>You have been assigned the task 'Will it Live?'.</p>
 
<p>This begins the 2nd task in the series '<a href="<!--server:x-->articles/article_page.php?article=q256&menustr=120000000000">Will it Live?</a>'</p> 1347 2011-02-26 08:00:55 2011-02-23 05:08:25 EQTC Editor Aanuvane 0 0 2011-02-26 08:00:33 EQTC Editor Aanuvane
257 CPS20_3 Coldain Prayer Shawl 2.0 #3 - Sewing it Forward <h4>Sewing it Forward </h4>
<p>This is the 3rd task in the Coldain Shawl 2.0 series. You must have previously completed '<a href="<!--server:x-->articles/article_page.php?article=q256&menustr=120000000000">Will it Live?</a>' and have a raw tailoring skill of 300 to request this task.</p>
 
<p>Quest NPC: Chamberlain Thoridain, Brell's Temple</p>
 
<h4>Task Steps:</h4>
<ul>
<li>Loot 3 Downy Gnoll Fur - Brell's Rest
<li>Loot 3 Downy Kobold Fur - Brell's Rest
<li>Loot 4 Pristine Mephit Wing Veins - Lichen Creep
<li>Loot 28 Loam Tainted Spider Silks - Fungal Forest
<li>Loot 10 Loam Tainted Slime - Fungal Forest
<li>Loot 4 Stonegrind Solvent - The Cooling Chamber
<li>Collect 12 Glacial Slush Water(s) - The Cooling Chamber
<li>Create 1 Woven Fur Padding using tradeskills - ALL
<li>Create 2 Wing Vein Boning using tradeskills - ALL
<li>Create 6 Underfoot Silk Thread using tradeskills - ALL
<li>Create 4 Underfoot Silk Swatch using tradeskills - ALL
<li>Create 1 Underfoot Silk Panel using tradeskills - ALL
<li>Deliver 1 Woven Fur Padding to Chamberlain Thoridain - Brell's Temple
<li>Deliver 2 Wing Vein Boning to Chamberlain Thoridain - Brell's Temple
<li>Deliver 1 Underfoot Silk Panel to Chamberlain Thoridain - Brell's Temple
<li>Wear your Revered Underfoot Prayer Shawl and speak with Chamberlain Thoridain - Brell's Temple
<li>Deliver your Revered Underfoot Prayer Shawl to Chamberlain Thoridain - Brell's Temple
</ul> 

<h4>Combines:</h4>

<h4>Details:</h4>
<p>You say, 'Hail, Chamberlain Thoridain'</p>
<p>Chamberlain Thoridain says 'While your skills with the Clay of Cosgrove were impressive, it has not moved the Creator. I must admit I have some doubts as to the chances of success but even so, we must try. Are you [willing] to test your skills in the third trial?'</p>
<p>You say, 'willing'</p>
<p>You have been assigned the task 'Sewing it Forward'.</p>
<p>Chamberlain Thoridain says 'Very good then. This trial will have you creating some necessary components of the shawls you have been receiving. These pieces will be used for any devoted followers who undertake these trials after you. Brell always looks kindly on those who help his devoted followers.'</p>
 
<p>This task starts out listing all the items you need to collect. Once you have collected all of the parts to make the items it unlocks the task steps for you to create the items. The task requires you to loot a certain amount, if you have completed that step and you fail a combine and need more, you can get the items from a vendor or another person if they are tradeable to replenish your supplies but you do have to do the initial looting. When you start the task, you will receive the Glacial Slush Water Collector.</p>
 
<p>Woven Fur Padding:</p>
<p>Downy Gnoll Fur drops off of any gnolls in Brell's Rest. They have a camp on the west side of the zone. Downy Kobold Fur drops off of any kobold in Brell's Rest. They have a camp on the east side of the zone. I would estimate it is about a 1 in 10 drop rate for these. When you start the task, you will receive the Glacial Slush Water Collector. This device is used to collect the glacial slush water from the cooling chamber. Go to the deepest part of the zone, where all the undead are by the lake. IVU is a big help. Find the largest iceberg in the lake, stand at the highest point, remove any levitation effects and jump off to the east into the water. Dive down slightly so that you are not floating near the surface, but do not swim all the way to the bottom. Click the Glacial Slush Water Collector and you will get 1 Glacial Slush Water. There is a 1 minute reuse timer on the collector so you will be sitting there for a little while. If you have found the right spot, and you removed any levitation effects, you should remain in the spot so you can repeat the process to collect all the waters you need. Note: THESE WATERS ARE TEMPORARY. Bring your Downy Gnoll and Kobold Furs down with you and combine them after you collect all the waters. 1 Downy Gnoll OR Kobold Fur + 2 Glacial Slush Waters will create Frost Shocked Gnoll or Kobold Furs. Chamberlain Thoridiain warns you that you will lose 1 of 4 of these combines so it can be helpful to bring extras. Once you have 3 Frost Shocked Downy Gnoll Furs and 3 Frost Shocked Downy Kobold Furs, combine them in your sewing kit to create the Woven Fur Padding.</p>
 
<p>Wing Vein Boning:</p>
<p>Pristine Mephit Wing Veins drop off of "a deranged mephit" in Lichen Creep. I would estimate these at a 1 in 10 drop rate. The deranged mephits can spawn in the place of any mephit in the zone so you may have to clear a bit to get enough drops. Stonegrind Solvent is a very common drop off of the goo's in the lower section of The Cooling Chamber near the zoneline to Pellucid Grotto. They are not hard to kill and the drops are fairly common. The solvent is no trade so you will need to camp these if you fail a combine and need more. The wing veins are tradeable so after looting your 4 you can get extras from others. Combine 2 of the wing veins with 2 of the solvents in your sewing kit to create the bonings. You need 2 bonings.</p>
 
<p>Underfoot Silk Panel:</p>
<p>Head to Fungal Forest. Find any spider mob, I found them most commonly on the west side of the zone closer to Pellucid Grotto. Any spider mob will drop between 1 and 5 Loam Tainted Spider Silks every time. These are fairly easy to collect and just require killing enough spiders. The Loam Tainted Slime drops from the oozes in the southern part of the zone. There are 2 versions of Loam Tainted Slime. The only one that will update the loot step of the task and can be used in the combines drop from a specific ooze "vigorous earth". These spawn in the Hungry Earth camp near Excrug Shrivstem. The slimes drop at about a 1 in 3 drop rate. The silks and the slimes are tradeable so you can get extras from others after fulfilling the loot requirement should you fail a combine. Once you have all the slimes and silks you can begin sewing the silks and swatches together. To make a thread, you need 2 silks and 1 slime. To make a swatch you need 1 thread, 4 silks, and 1 slime. To make the panel you need 4 swatches and 2 threads. This totals to 28 silks and 10 slimes if you have no failures.</p>
 
<p>Turn in the Woven Fur Padding, the Wing Vein Bonings, and the Underfoot Silk Panel to Chamberlain Thoridain. Put your Revered Underfoot Prayer Shawl on and hail Chamberlain Thoridain.</p>
 
<p>You say, 'Hail, Chamberlain Thoridain'</p>
<p>Chamberlain Thoridain says 'Great. Give me your Revered Underfoot Prayer Shawl, and I will give you your next shawl.'</p>
 
<p>Hand in your shawl and receive <!--item_linkedname:37581--> and 5aa.</p>
 
<p>You say, 'Hail, Chamberlain Thoridain'</p>
<p>Chamberlain Thoridain says 'Ah yes. Very good. Service to others, and sharing of your craft is important to Brell.'</p>
 
<p>Chamberlain Thoridain says 'The craftsmanship of the previous pieces you created was outstanding. Even though nothing has changed with Brell, we will press on. Are you prepared to [accept] the fourth trial?'</p>
<p>You say, 'accept'</p>
<p>You have been assigned the task 'Bring Him a Brew!'</p>
 
<p>This starts the 4th task in the series, '<a href="<!--server:x-->articles/article_page.php?article=q258&menustr=120000000000">Bring Him a Brew!</a>'</p> 1347 2011-02-26 08:06:06 2011-02-24 09:38:30 EQTC Editor Aanuvane 0 0 2011-02-26 08:03:53 EQTC Editor Aanuvane
258 CPS20_4 Coldain Prayer Shawl 2.0 #4:   Bring him a Brew <h4>Bring Him a Brew!</h4> 
<p>This is the 4th task in the Coldain Shawl 2.0 series. You must have previously completed '<a href="<!--server:x-->articles/article_page.php?article=q257&menustr=120000000000">Sewing it Forward</a>' and have a raw brewing skill of 300 to request this task.</p>
 
<p>Quest NPC: Chamberlain Thoridain, Brell's Temple</p>
 
<h4>Task Steps:</h4>
<ul>
<li>Create 1 Brell's Best using tradeskills - ALL
<li>Speak with Thoridain and show him your success making Brell's Best - Brell's Temple
<li>Collect 1 Brell's Rest Water Sample - Brell's Rest
<li>Collect 1 Cooling Chamber Water Sample - The Cooling Chamber
<li>Collect 1 Underquarry Water Sample - The Underquarry
<li>Collect 1 Foundation Water Sample - The Foundation
<li>Collect 1 Pellucid Grotto Water Sample - Pellucid Grotto
<li>Collect 1 Arthicrex Water Sample - Arthicrex
<li>Collect 1 Fungal Forest Water Sample - Fungal Forest
<li>Create 1 Pure Underfoot Spirits using tradeskills - ALL
<li>Collect 1 Jelly of the Cliknar Queen(s) - Arthicrex
<li>Inform the Chamberlain that you have acquired the Jelly of the Cliknar Queen - Brell's Temple
<li>Loot 1 Sacred Cask of Brell - ALL
<li>Create 1 Brell's Mystical Brew using tradeskills - ALL
<li>Deliver 1 Magical Water Collection Jar to Chamberlain Thoridain - Brell's Temple
<li>Deliver 1 Brell's Mystical Brew to Chamberlain Thoridain - Brell's Temple
<li>Wear your Sacred Underfoot Prayer Shawl and speak with Chamberlain Thoridain - Brell's Temple
<li>Deliver your Sacred Underfoot Prayer Shawl to Chamberlain Thoridain - Brell's Temple
 </ul>
<h4>Combines:</h4>
<table  cellpadding="2" hspace="10" bordercolor="#400000" vspace="1" border="2" cellspacing="0">
<tr>
<th class="intable"><i>Item</i></th>
<th class="intable"><i>Recipe</i></th>
<th class="intable"><i>Trivial</i></th>
</tr>
<tr>
<td class="intable"><!--item_op:32900..0..1..1--></td>
<td class="intable" valign="top"><!--recipe:31665--></td>
<td class="intable" valign="top"><!--recipe_trivial:31665--></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td class="intable"><!--item_op:37520..0..1..1--></td>
<td class="intable" valign="top"><!--recipe:37033--></td>
<td class="intable" valign="top"><!--recipe_trivial:37033--></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td class="intable"><!--item_op:37528..0..1..1--></td>
<td class="intable" valign="top"><!--recipe:37034--></td>
<td class="intable" valign="top"><!--recipe_trivial:37034--></td>
</tr>
</table>
<h4>Details:</h4>
<p>You say, 'Hail, Chamberlain Thoridain'</p>
<p>Chamberlain Thoridain says 'The craftsmanship of the previous pieces you created was outstanding. Even though nothing has changed with Brell, we will press on. Are you prepared to [accept] the fourth trial?'</p>
<p>You say, 'accept'</p>
<p>You have been assigned the task 'Bring Him a Brew!'</p>
 
<p>The first step in this task is to create a Brell's Best. This recipe is explained in the book, Brewing Brell's Best, sold on the Useful Automated Vendor in Brell's Rest. Return to Thoridain and hail him,</p>
 
<p>You say, 'Hail, Chamberlain Thoridain'</p>
<p>Your task 'Bring Him a Brew!' has been updated.</p>
<p>Chamberlain Thoridain says 'I see your talent at brewing is not understated. Hold on to that brew since we'll be using it as a base. Now we will begin your trial in earnest. Here is a magical water sampling jar. Travel to the areas I have indicated and collect a sample of water from each. There is likely only one suitable water supply in each area so you may need to do some searching. Be sure you do not lose the jar as I will want it back when you are done.'</p>
 
<p>You receive Magical Water Collection Jar. It is an inventory clickable item, 0.5 sec cast time that will collect water samples and duplicate itself, allowing unlimited collecting of samples.</p>
 
<p>Now you must travel to each of the zones indicated and collect a sample of water.</p>
<ul>
<li>In Brell's Rest, the steaming pool with the elementals is the proper location. Run in/near/there and click the collection jar. You will receive a sample. Clicking the jar does remove invisibility when you receive the water sample. Simply wait for the pather to move away and you can find a spot in the middle near the cooling chamber zone pit.</li>
<li>In the Cooling Chamber, the location is the lake all the way at the bottom with the undead. Run with invis/ivu down to the lake and find a spot in the water with no mobs around.</li>
<li>In the Underquarry, the location is the small lake in the main quest NPC room near the genari. Stay on the opposite side of the water from them and you can collect the sample without aggro.</li>
<li>In the Foundation, you will need to head east from the zone in to the next section and there is a small lake with some autarchians and baelorats around it.</li>
<li>In Pellucid Grotto, the lake in the far northwest corner of the zone is where you need to go where the memory crystals spawn around the lake. Move towards the middle of the lake to find a safe spot.</li>
<li>In Arthicrex, there is a small puddle in the ravine near the Underquarry zone in. There are 2-3 cliknar and 2-3 oozes that spawn near there that can see invis, be careful.</li>
<li>In Fungal Forest, there is a small pond near the east end of the zone with mephits all around it. Rarely will a mephit ganger see through invis so simply approach from a different side from them and can collect the sample near the middle of the lake.</li>
</ul> 
<p>Once you have all of the water samples, you need to create the Pure Underfoot Spirits. To do this, combine the 7 water samples you have collected in a brew barrel with a cask, barley, and yeast. Once you have this, you now must collect the Jelly of the Cliknar Queen. This is a ground spawn in Arthicrex deep in the Hive in the northern end of the zone. Go up the switchbacks to enter the hive area, be careful there are see-invis mobs along this path. Once at the top, go into the hive and down towards the bottom. The very bottom room has 2 tables with colored jars. Going up from the bottom to the 2nd path from the bottom leads to another room where the Hive Nurse spawns there are some additional tables with colored jars stacked on them. The ground spawn is ON one of the tables and it is a large vial that is yellow and sparklie. Several see-invis mobs are in the room as well as other trash mobs. Nothing sees through SoS. Once you have reached the room, either clear the mobs, or use some form of invulnerability to run in and grab the ground spawn is the best suggestion I can give. It was not easy to obtain. After you have the jelly, you need to return to Chamberlain Thoridain and speak to him.</p>
 
<p>You say, 'Hail, Chamberlain Thoridain'</p>
<p>Your task 'Bring Him a Brew!' has been updated.</p>
<p>Chamberlain Thoridain says 'I am glad to see you were able to procure this jelly. That was no easy task I'm sure. The last thing we will need is a Sacred Cask of Brell. We only use them for the most sacred brews. They are kept in cold storage in Kernagir. You should speak to Brewmeister Stiegl about obtaining one.</p>
 
<p>Now you need to head to Kernagir and find Brewmeister Stiegl.</p>
 
<p>You say, 'Hail, Brewmeister Stiegl'</p>
<p>Brewmeister Stiegl says 'What do you want?'</p>
<p>You say, 'sacred cask of brell'</p>
<p>Brewmeister Stiegl says 'Oh yeah? Well I am not in the giving mood today. Get'em!'</p>
 
<p>When you say the key phrase to him, the normal mobs in his room will despawn and 5 "a coldain brewer" will spawn and attack you. You need to clear these mobs and then Brewmeister Stiegl will become active and attack. Defeat him and he will drop the Sacred Cask of Brell. They hit like normal Kernagir trash mobs. Upon the death of Brewmeister Stiegl, the normal trash mobs in the room respawn.</p>
 
<p>Now that you have the cask you are ready to create Brell's Mythical Brew. To do this you combine the Sacred Cask of Brell with the Pure Underfoot Spirits, Brell's Best, and Jelly of the Cliknar Queen, as well as Yeast, Malt, and Hops in a brew barrel. Then you take this mythical brew along with the water collection jar back to Chamberlain Thoridain. Hand in the jar, then the brew, and then wear your shawl, hail Chamberlain again and then turn your shawl in to receive the Blessed Sanctified Underfoot Prayer Shawl.</p>
 
<p>Upon handing in the Water Collection Jar:</p>
<p>Chamberlain Thoridain says 'Thank you for returning this. It's very valuable and we would not want to be without it.'</p>
 
<p>Upon handing in the Brell's Mythical Brew:</p>
<p>Chamberlain Thoridain says 'This is incredible work! Never have I seen a brew as potent as this. I hope it will have some effect on the creator.'</p>

<p>Hand your Sacred Underfoot Prayer Shawl to Chamberlain Thoridain.</p>
<p>Chamberlain Thoridain says 'You have done the brewers of Underfoot proud with your accomplishments today. Here is your new shawl with any augments you may have had in it.</p>

259 CPS20_5 Coldain Prayer Shawl 2.0 #5 - I Hope You Can Hear This <h4>I Hope You Can Hear This </h4>
<p>This is the 5th task in the Coldain Shawl 2.0 series. You must have previously completed '<a href="<!--server:x-->articles/article_page.php?article=q258&menustr=120000000000">Bring Him a Brew!</a>' and have a raw fletching skill of 300 to request this task.</p>
 
<p>Quest NPC: Chamberlain Thoridain, Brell's Temple</p>
 
<h4>Task Steps:</h4>
<ul>
<li>Collect 2 Fallen Branch(es) from somewhere in the Underfoot ? ALL</li>

<li>Create 6 Wood Panel using tradeskills - Brell's Temple</li>
<li>Create 1 Ornate Trim using tradeskills - Brell's Temple</li>
<li>Create 1 Rune Case using tradeskills - Brell's Temple</li>

<h4>Details:</h4>
<p>You say, 'Hail, Chamberlain Thoridain'</p>
<p>Chamberlain Thoridain says 'Your brew was truly potent. I believe I saw some glimmer of recognition from Brell when I gave it to him. We may be getting through to him after all! We must move forward with the next trial. Are you [prepared]?</p>
<p>You say, 'prepared'</p>
<p>You have been assigned the task 'I Hope You Can Hear This'</p>
<p>Chamberlain Thoridain says 'Good. Given the reaction to your brew, Brell may be receptive to further input. You will attempt to create the sacred prayer runes of Brell. Given the sacred nature of these runes, I am sure it will have some effect. Off you go!?</p>
 
<p>The first step is to find a place that has some fallen trees. The particular place you are looking for is in Pellucid Grotto in the northeast section of the zone in the cliknar area. Upon approaching the appropriate place, you will receive an emote that will cause the ground spawns to appear. There are some see invis cliknar in the area you will want to avoid. The ground spawns look like sticks with a couple green leaves on the ground around the downed trees. The fallen branches do not stack. You will need to collect 6 branches even though the task only calls for 2 for the first update. [2 branches for the tool, 3 branches to make the 6 wood panels (yield of 2), and 1 branch for the ornate trim] The ground spawns will respawn if you stay in the area so you can find one or 2 spots and just wait for them to pop again.</p>
 
<p>Intact Greken Spines drop from any greken model in Underfoot. Greken models are the nestlings in the lava in Brell's Rest and are also found in the lavapool in Convorteum. In Brell's Rest I was experiencing a drop rate of roughly 1 in 10. In Convorteum I had a much better drop rate closer to 1 in 3. I do not know if it was just good/bad luck with the RNG but I would estimate it is probably a 1 in 5 global drop rate for that NPC model. The spines are no drop and stack to 4. Combine 2 fallen branches and the 4 intact greken spines to create the Rune Carving Tools. This combine, and all the fletching combines for this task, can ONLY be done on the fletching table in Brell's Temple in the main room where Brell Serilis wanders. Now that you have your Rune Carving Tools, you need to find something to make the runes out of. Smooth Stones drop fairly commonly from oozes in Arthicrex, Fungal Forest, and Pellucid Grotto. I simply went back to the Hungry Earth camp in Fungal Forest and killed the oozes there and was not long to collect the 6 stones. Back to Brell's Temple.</p>
 
<p>You say, 'Hail, Chamberlain Thoridain'</p>
<p>Your task 'I Hope You Can Hear This' has been updated.</p>
<p>Chamberlain Thoridain says 'I see you managed to create your rune carving tools and find some suitable stones. You are ready to begin carving the runes. Here are the patterns for our six prayer runes. Simply carve the pattern into the stone using your tools. Remember, this must be done using the fletching table here in Brell's workshop.'</p>
 
<p>Chamberlain Thoridain gives you the 6 rune patterns. They do not stack. The fletching table is right in that room, combine a stone with each of the patterns and your carving tools. The tools are returned on success. Once you have crafted all 6 of the runes you need to speak with Chamberlain Thoridain again. It updates the task but there is no dialogue. The task window now provides you with the recipes for the wood panels and the ornate trim. One fallen branch in the fletching table yields 2 wood panels. Create the 6 wood panels and then the ornate trim using the last of your 6 fallen branches and your carving tools. Now you can fashion the Rune Case using the wood panels, ornate trim, and your carving tools. The Rune Case does consume the carving tools. The Rune Case is a container so you will need to have a top level inventory spot available when you make this combine. Place the 6 Sacred Prayer Runes in the Rune Case and hit combine to create the Case of Runes. Hand the Case of Runes into Chamberlain Thoridain. Wear your Blessed Sanctified Underfoot Prayer Shawl and hail him and then turn your Blessed Sanctified Underfoot Prayer Shawl in.</p>
 
<p>Your task 'I Hope You Can Hear This' has been updated.</p>
<p>You say, 'Hail, Chamberlain Thoridain'</p>
<p>Chamberlain Thoridain says 'Great. Give me your Blessed Sanctified Underfoot Prayer Shawl, and I will give you your next shawl.'</p>
<p>Your task 'I Hope You Can Hear This' has been updated.</p>
<p>Your task 'I Hope You Can Hear This' has been updated.</p>
<p>You have shown your skill in carving the sacred prayer runes.</p>
<p>You gain experience!!</p>
<p>Chamberlain Thoridain says 'The runes printed perfectly! Do not worry as the sacred ink will never wear or fade. Here is your new shawl with any augments you may have had. '</p>
 
<p>At this point you will receive your new shawl.</p>
<p>Casters: <!--item_linkedname:37584-->
<br>Melee: <!--item_linkedname:37585--></p>
 
<p>You say, 'Hail, Chamberlain Thoridain'</p>
<p>Chamberlain Thoridain says 'It's working! I'm sure I saw Him smile when you were creating the sacred runes. We must move quickly if we are to take advantage of this. Shall we [commence] the sixth task?'</p>
<p>You say, 'commence'</p>
<p>You have been assigned the task 'Honoring the Elements'.</p>
<p>Chamberlain Thoridain says 'This task is the one of the most sacred rites in the temple. You must honor the elements of creation. You will begin by collection the essences of creation. Normally these could be obtained peacefully but the current chaos in Underfoot requires you get them by force. Brell will understand the sacrifices were necessary. Return as soon as you have what you need.'</p>

<h4>Details:</h4>
 
<p>You say, 'Hail, Chamberlain Thoridain'</p>
<p>Chamberlain Thoridain says 'It's working! I'm sure I saw Him smile when you were creating the sacred runes. We must move quickly if we are to take advantage of this. Shall we [commence] the sixth task?'</p>
<p>You say, 'commence'</p>
<p>You have been assigned the task 'Honoring the Elements'.</p>
<p>Chamberlain Thoridain says 'This task is the one of the most sacred rites in the temple. You must honor the elements of creation. You will begin by collection the essences of creation. Normally these could be obtained peacefully but the current chaos in Underfoot requires you get them by force. Brell will understand the sacrifices were necessary. Return as soon as you have what you need.'</p>
 
<p>Collect all of the Essences. These ARE pre-lootable. Once you have all 35, you return to Chamberlain Thoridain and hail him to get the instructions on how to craft the gems.</p>
<ul>
<li>Reason - drops from any bellikos</li>
<li>Will - drops from any cliknar</li>
<li>Passion - drops from any gnome</li>
<li>Substance - drops from any golem</li>
<li>Instinct - drops from any greken</li>
<li>Vitality - drops from any genari</li>
<li>Chaos - drops from any apexus</li>
</ul>
<p>One you have all the essences, return to Chamberlain Thoridain in Brell's Temple</p>
<p>You say, 'Hail, Chamberlain Thoridain'</p>
<p>Chamberlain Thoridain says 'Very good. The next part of the trial will require access to the Font Chamber. If you have not yet assisted Gotonur in creating a keystone, you should speak to him now. If you already have the keystone then let us [proceed].'<p>
<p>You say, 'proceed'</p>
<p>Your task 'Honoring the Elements' has been updated.</p>
<p>Chamberlain Thoridain says 'First you will need to make Cosgrove Amalgam by mixing some mercury and cosgrove powder. Then you will use this amalgam to fuse the essences you collected into a solid gem. However, to do this you will need the energy of the corresponding elemental font. Simply stand in the appropriate font for whichever essences you are attempting to fuse. If you are successful, you will create a raw gem from those essences. After that everything else should be quite simple.'<p>


<p>To craft the Cosgrove Amalgam, you need to combine a Mercury with a Cosgrove Powder. The amalgam does not stack. You will need 7 of these. To combine the essences with the amalgam you must be standing in the proper Font. The Fonts are located in the locked room inside Brell's Temple. To reach this room, you must be carrying the Keystone reward from the Brell's Temple mission and it will open the door just north of the main central room where Brell Serilis is located. Inside you will see 7 colored spheres over some bowls. Those are the Fonts. The color of the essences corresponds with the color Font you need to be standing in to complete the combine. I recommend dropping levitation effects, walking up the front side of the stand and dropping into the bowl of the proper Font. You will need a collapsed or reinforced jewelry kit to make these 6 item combines. Combine the 5 essences with an amalgam in the proper font. If you are not close enough to the bowl, you will receive a message saying you must be closer to the font of XXX depending on which essence/color you are trying to make. Once you create the uncut gems in the Fonts, you will need to cut them. Oval cut tools and a Jewelers Glass in your JC kit. Once you have all 7 Brilliant gems, you will need to combine them with an Enchanted bar of Cosgrite on the Jewelry Making Bench located in the main room with Brell Serilis. Then you simply need to hand in the Clasp of the Elements to Chamberlain Thoridain, wear your shawl and hail him and then turn in your Revered Sanctified Underfoot Prayer Shawl.</p>
 
<p>Upon completion of this task you will receive:</p>
<p>Casters: <!--item_linkedname:37582-->
<br>Melee: <!--item_linkedname:37583--></br></p>
 
<p>This also will lead into the 7th task of the series <a href="<!--server:x-->articles/article_page.php?article=q261&menustr=120000000000">The Temper of Silver</a>

261 CPS20_7 Coldain Prayer Shawl 2.0 #7: The Temper of Silver <h4>The Temper of Silver</h4>
<p>This is the 7th task in the Coldain Shawl 2.0 Series.  You must have previously completed '<a href="<!--server:x-->articles/article_page.php?article=q260&menustr=120000000000">Honoring the Elements</a>' and have a raw blacksmithing skill of 300 to request this task.  You must also have completed Tier 9 Underfoot progressions and Convorteum Progression, including the Keystone from Brell's Temple progression.</p>

<p>Quest NPC: Chamberlain Thoridain, Brell's Temple</p>
<h4>Task Steps:</h4>
<ul>
<li>Collect 2 Raw Underfoot Silver - ALL</li>
<li>Collect 1 Raw Underfoot Copper - ALL</li>
<li>Create 2 Refined Underfoot Silver using tradeskills - ALL</li>
<li>Create 1 Refined Underfoot Copper using tradeskills - ALL</li>
<li>Create 1 Brell Silver Using Tradeskills - ALL</li>
<li>Deliver 1 Brell Silver to a clockwork magma meter MCMXCIC</li>
<li>Escort a clockwork magma meter MCMXCIX to it's first testing point 0/1 (The Convorteum)</li>
<li>Escort a clockwork magma meter MCMXCIX to it's second testing point 0/1 (The Convorteum)</li>
<li>Escort a clockwork magma meter MCMXCIX to it's third testing point 0/1 (The Convorteum)</li>

<h4>Details</h4>
<p>You say, 'Hail, Chamberlain Thoridain'</p>

<p>Chamberlain Thoridain says 'Your honoring of the elements was a success! Brell seemed to be watching you as you worked. However, I have only one trial left. I hope it will be enough. Will you [undertake] the seventh trial?' </p>
<p>You say, 'undertake'</p>
<p>Chamberlain Thoridain says 'Excellent! You will create some of the finest and hardest silver you have ever seen. This silver is blessed from the fires of the heart of the underfoot itself. You will make a filigree to use in the shawls, making them themselves an item of devotion to Brell.'</p>
<p>You have been assigned the task 'The Temper of Silver'.</p>

<p>When you request the task, you are given the Silver Filigree Pattern that you will need for the final combine.  At this point you need to go to Underquarry and kill a cliknar mine worker to get two Raw Underfoot Silvers and a burynai plotter drops the Raw Underfoot Copper.  Once you have these, combine them in a forge to make the refined metals and then combine them to make the Brell Silver.  At this point you are ready for the shawl walk in Convorteum.</p>
<p>Up the tunnel near the zone in is the clockwork npc.  Hail him and you can turn in the Brell Silver to begin.  The clockwork will walk down the path towards the field and test the lava in several places.  He will stop to attack any mob that gets near him as well.  He does decent dps and can tank a couple mobs at a time.  But if you let him run off on his own, he will die and you will have to recollect the drops.  Bring some friends and escort the gnome around to the 5 locations.  To begin, say ?start?.  At any time, you can say ?stop? and the clockwork will stay in place.  Saying ?continue? will make him resume on his way towards his next point.  Locations the clockwork walks to:</p>
<li>at Loc [-870,692,-76]</li>
<li>at Loc [-1195,595,-76]</li>
<li>at Loc [-978,665,-76]</li>
<li>at Loc [-671,704,-76]</li>
<li>at Loc [-466,735,-76]</li>

<p>When he reaches each spot, he will stop for a minute or so and then the task will update when he begins to move again.  At 3 of the 5 locations, while he is waiting at the lava, 2 mobs will spawn named, a ravenous greken.  Hit for about the same as normal Convorteum trash mobs.   Once he reaches his starting point, you will receive the Heart of the Underfoot used in the final combine.  There is a time limit to the walk that if you get an emote about the power level of the clockwork that is a warning about the timer.  Next, head back to Brell?s Temple and use the forge around the center room and combine the Heart of the Underfoot with the pattern to create the final item to turn in.  Turn the item into Chamberlain Thoridain and then hail.  Wear your shawl and hail then turn your Sacred Sanctified shawl in to receive the Blessed Serilis Prayer Shawl.</p>
<p>You say, ?Hail, Chamberlain Thoridain,?</p>
<p>Chamberlain Thoridan says, ?How wonderful.  Brell himself spoke to you.  Though he has not stopped in his task, it brings me great hope that he will soon stop what he is doing and go back to his normal self.  You have done more than I could ever hope for, and I thank you.  If you have a very large group of friends, there is one more thing that may bering even more of Brell?s attention.  I will not think less of you if you cannot complete this task.  If you are [interested] bring me the head of the creature that has caused Brell to become distracted.  Also, if you are interested, you may [exchange your shawl] for a similar version of equal power.
</p>

71 EQTC:Quests:Luclin:ProgressiveTa Shar Vahl - Progressive Tailoring Quests <p>
Hand Broker Fahaar in Shar Vahl your <a href="<!--server:x-->articles/article_page.php?article=q42&menustr=120070000000">personal acrylia slate</a>. He will give you a 4-slot Young Hopperhide Sack (lore, no drop).
</p>
<p>
Combine 4 young rockhopper hides (no drop off young rockhoppers, from the pit surrounding Shar Vahl) and return the filled bag to Broker Fahaar to receive a leather cord (no drop) and a stretched hopperhide. Repeat. Return 4 cords to and receive a <b>Vah Shir skinning knife</b>.
</p>
<p>
Make a <a href="<!--server:x-->items/show_item.php?item=5731">rough belt strap</a> and give it and your Vah Shir skinning knife to Broker Fahaar to receive your <b>Vah Shir needle set</b>.
</p>
<p>
Next, bring Broker Fahaar a <a href="<!--server:x-->items/show_item.php?item=5733">black chitin belt</a> and a <a href="<!--server:x-->items/show_item.php?item=5734">bone beaded belt</a> plus your Vah Shir needle set to receive an <b>acrylia needle</b>.
</p>
<p>
Broker Fahaar will then ask you to make him <a href="<!--server:x-->items/show_item.php?item=5735">owlbear feathered leggings</a>. Once you have made the leggings, and give them and your acrylia need to him, he will give you a 6-slot (no drop, of course) container to fill with six <a href="<!--server:x-->items/show_item.php?item=5738">owlbear tunics</a>. He will also upgrade your needle to an <b>acrylia thimble & needle set</b> (As always, make sure you have room for the extra container in your inventory.)
</p>
<p>
Combine 6 owlbear tunics in the container, and hand the result to Elder Hortitosh in the Bard guild in the Shar Vahl Palace.
</p>
<blockquote>
<p>
Elder Hymnist Hortitosh says 'These are finely crafted indeed, ____. Merchant Fahaar told me you were quite the prodigy, but don't tell him I told you that. Take this receipt and show it to Fahaar and tell him the king is quite pleased with both your work, and his teaching!' 
</p>
</blockquote>
<p>
Bring the receipt to Broker Fahaar and he will respond with the following.
</p>
<blockquote>
<p>
Broker Fahaar says 'Well done, ______. You have done very well and the king is pleased. You have been a great help to me filling that order for the king. Here, take this jerkin and wear it with pride. All who see it will know that you are an accomplished tailor and a friend of Fareen!' 
</p>
</blockquote>
<p>
He will then give you a Sleek Sonic Wolfhide Tunic (AC 16, STR5, STA4, CHA 10; WAR, BST, ROG, BRD, SHM; VAH, BAR, TRL, OGR, IKS no drop).
